36a6(phal chen): dag par 'gyur te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sems can gyi gtso bo 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan na bzhugs pas yang dag par dgongs pa dang / 'das pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i grogs kyis/ dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa dang
36a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi ya / par gzung ba la mkhas pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen la yang dag par brten pa dang / mos pa dang / brtson 'grus dang / bag yod pa la rab tu gnas pa dang / cho tha dad pa thams
36a8(phal chen): cad la tha mi dad par rtogs pa dang / snying rje'i byin gyis brlabs shin tu che ba dang / chos thams cad yang dag par ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par lta ba'i shes rab kyis pha rol tu phyin pa mngon par bsgrub pa dang / thabs
36b1(phal chen): la mkhas pa rnam par dpyod pa'i spyong ba dang / sbyor ba thams cad la de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs kyi rjesu 'brang ba dag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ rnam pa bcu po dadag gis/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis spyod pa'i/ 
36b2(phal chen): dkyil 'khor yongasu sbyangs par bya'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras de la byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam rnam par dag pa bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ skyo ba med par sems can gyi khams yongasu smin par bya ba'i
36b3(phal chen): smon lam dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba sna tshogs bsags pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams yongasu dag par bya ba'i smon lam dang / lus dang srog gis bsngo zhing dam pa'i chos yongasu 'dzin pa'i smon lam dang / ye shes kyi sgo
36b4(phal chen): rnang par dbang pa khong du chud pas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing la 'jug pa'i spor lam dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad dang gcisu me dpas/ tshul gcig gi rgyud du 'gro ba'i smon lam dang / de bzhin sa
36b5(phal chen): pa'i sgo la 'jug pas chos thams cad khong du chud ba'i smod lam dang / mos pa rnam par sbyangs pas blta na ngon yod pa'i smon la ma dang / phyi ma'i mthar byin gyis brlabs pas bskal par gnas
36b6(phal chen): smon lam dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i theg pa'i rgyan rnam pa thams cad kyi sgo nas/ rnam par sbyangs pa'i smon lam dag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni de ltar smon
36b7(phal chen): lam rnam par sbyong ngo // de dag rnam pa bcus smon lam yong su rdzogs par byed/ bcu gang zhe na/ yongasu skyo ba med pa dang / rgya chen po mngon par bsgrub pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' smon lam khyad par du 'jam
36b8(phal chen): pa rnams kyi rje su 'jug pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams gzham na bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi ning thos nas/ rang gi spod la mi du mngon par bsgrub pa dang / bsapa pa phyi ma'i mtha'i bur thug
37a1(phal chen): pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad yongasu smin par bya bar gtugs pa'i smon lam chen po dang ldan pa dang / bskal pa thams cad gnas pas mi 'jigs pa dang / sdug bsngal thams
37a2(phal chen): cad kyis ji mi sbam pa dang / bde ba thams cad la ye mi brdab pa dang / bsam pa mnyam pa med pa'i rnam par thar pa yongasu srung ba dag ste/ de dag smon lam chen po de ltar yongs spyod zhing yong su rdzogs par byed pa'i tshe/ 
37a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas mthong ba'i gter zang mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo// gzungs 'khrul pa med pa'i gter zang mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo// smon lam zad mi shes pas chos thams cad shin tu rtogs pa'i gzungs
37a4(phal chen): kyang rab tu 'thob bo// snying rje cher pos 'gro ba thams cad yongs spyod ba'i gter zang mi gas pa 'ang rab tu 'thob bo// ting 'dzin gyi rgyud kyi gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo// 'gro ba thams cad
37a5(phal chen): tshim par bya ba'i bsod rnams kyi gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu thongab bo// chos thams cad yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du byam/ pa'i ye shes kyi gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo// rnam par
37a6(phal chen): smin pa la gnas pa mngon par bsgrung pa'i gter zang mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo// sangs rgyas kyi byir gyis brlangs mtha' yas pa'i gter zang mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo// 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' dang
37a7(phal chen): dbus med par gtogs pa la 'jug pa'i gter zad mi shes pa'ang rab tu 'thob bo// de ltar gter rab tu thob cing bsod nams dang / ye shes kyi tshogs zad mi shes pa dang ldan pa de dag ye shes chen po'i dkyil
37a8(phal chen): 'khor yongasu dag pas/ sems can rnams la bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du chos kyi gter gyi sbyin pa bye// de la rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams sems can rnams kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du/ 
37b1(phal chen): ji ltar 'jug cen/ sbyor ba ji lta bu rgyu ba dang / rgyu dang rkyen ji lta ba dang / sems dang sems las byung ba'i spyor ba ji lta ba las sems can rnams kyi bsam paji lta ba bzhin du 'jug ste/ de dag de ltar bsam pa la
37b2(phal chen): zhugs pa rnams sems can rnams kyis bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du shes shing / chos yang dag par stor te/ nga ngag 'dod chags kyi bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir/ mi sdug pa yang dag par ston to// zhe sdang gi bsam
37b3(phal chen): ba rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir/ byams pa chen po'i sbyor ba yang dag par ston to// gti mug gi bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir/ chos rnam par 'byed pa la mkhas par yang ga co to cha mnyam pa rnam par bzlog pa
37b4(phal chen): phyir/ ye shes kyi khyad par dang ldan pa'i chos kyi sgo yang dag par ston to// 'khor ba'i bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir/ sdug bsngal gsum dang ldan pa yang dag par ston to// gnas kyi bsam pa rnam par
37b5(phal chen): bzlog pa'i phyir/ garas med pa'i chos kyi sgo yang dag par stor to// nub pa'i ngasam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir/ rgyan chen 'i yul yang dag par ston to// bdag gi nga rgyal gyis bcom
37b6(phal chen): bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir/ chos kyi mnyar ba nyid yang dag par ston to// g.yo dang sgras mi mnyam pa'i bsam pa rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa mnyam pa nyid dang / zhi ba
37b7(phal chen): gnas kyi bsam pa mngon par bsgrub pa yang dag par ston to// de dag ni de ltar sems can rnams la bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du chos kyi gter yang dag par ston te/ de yang don dbyer med pa yang dag par ston to// 
37b8(phal chen): ge'i ra bas sbyor bas sbyar bas yang dag par ston to// shes pa rnam par dbye bas yang dag par ston to// bstan pa snga phyi ma 'dres pas yang dag par ston to// chos kyi tshul dang tshul ma yin pa'i bye brag dbyer med
38a1(phal chen): pas yang dag par ston to// mtshar nyid kyi phyag rgya rnam par mi 'khrugs pas yang dag par ston to// chos rab tu dgod pa rgyun chad pa med pas yang dag par ston to// mtha' yas pa
38a2(phal chen): spang bas yang dag par ston to// the tsom thams cad shin tu gcad pa'i phyir yang dag par ston to// dbang po'i rgyud la 'jug pa'i phyir yang dag par ston to// de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag rgya la dgod par gzhol bas yang
38a3(phal chen): dag par ston to// yang dag pa'i mtha' mtshan nyid med pa rnam par mi 'khrugs pas yang dag par ston to// chos kyi dbyings la yang dag par gzhol bas yang dag par ston to// chos kyi rnga yang dag par brdungs pas yang
38a4(phal chen): dag par ston to// gnas thams cad yang dag par spang bas yang dag par ston to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad rjesu dran pa mi gtong bas yang dag par ston to// tshig dang skad dang sgra dang ngag gi lam thams nad
38a5(phal chen): mnyam pa nyid la mi gnas pas yang dag par ston to// rnam par mi rtog pa'i dbyings kyi rjesu 'gro bas yang dag par ston to// dpe thams cad rnam par dgod
38a6(phal chen): pas rgyud dang mi 'gal bar brtan par bya bas yang dag par ston to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor rang gi lus su sems pa la yang dag par gzhol bas yang dag par ston to// de ltar sen
38a7(phal chen): la chos yang dag par ston cing rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad bar chos kyi nan tan gyi mtshan nyid kyi rjesu 'brang ba dang / rang gi don cing tshugs par byed pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa'i phyogs mi gtong bas rgyan chen po'i pha rol tu
38a8(phal chen): phyin pa'i theg pa yang dag par sgrub bo/ de la'ang sems can thams cad tshim par bya ba dang / yo byad kyis yongasu bsnyung ba dang / sbyor ba mnyam par yong su gtong bas/ sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongasug par bya// 
38b1(phal chen): yang dag par blangs pa mi gtong ba dang / gnas med pa dang / nga rgyal med pas tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongasu dag par byed// nyes pa thams cad khyadrug stong pa dang / sems can thams cad kyis mi 'khrugs pa
38b2(phal chen): dang / mnyam pa nyid la gzhol ba dang / mthon dman med pa dang / zang mi shes pa'i sa mnyam par 'dzin pas/ bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongasu dag par byed// brtsam pa chen por rtsom pa dang / brtsam pa thams cad
38b3(phal chen): 'azhub pa med pa dang / sbyor ba phyir mi ldog pa dang / yid la byed pa phyir mi 'gyur ba dang / mthu mtha' yas pa dang / stobs la thub pa med pa dang / sngon du 'dong ba mi 'phrog pa dang / dad pa'i mthu chen po dang / blang
38b4(phal chen): ba dang de rab med pa'i tsho gos thams cad yongasu rgyas par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i spo lams pa med pa la yang dag par 'a jug pas/ brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongasu dag par
38b5(phal chen): byed do// 'dod ba'i yon tan thams cad kyi 'du 'ji yongasu spyong ba dang / mi 'bral ba dang / rim gyis bsam gtan dang / ting 'dzin mngon par bsgrub pa dang / gnas med cing blang ba med pa shin/ 
38b6(phal chen): rtogs pa dang / nyon mongs pa thams cad rab tu sel ba dang / ting 'dzin sgo mtha' yas pa mngon par bsgrub pa dang / mngon par shes pa chen pos rnam par 'phrul ba'i rjesu 'gro ba dang / rim gyis rnam par spong ba
38b7(phal chen): ting 'dzin gyi sgo la rab tu 'jug pa dang / ting 'dzin gcig la sgo mtha' yas pa rab tu 'jug pa dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi spyod yul thams cad shes pa dang / de'i yul gyi rjes rab tu zhugs pa dang / ting 'dzin dang
38b8(phal chen): spobs par 'jug pa thams cad ye shes kyi phyag rgya mi 'khrugs pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i sa la nye bar gyur pas/ bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa yong su dag par byod// sangs rgyas kyi chos thams
39a1(phal chen): mnyan pa dang / gzung ba dang / blang ba dang / bcang ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad bsnyen bkur bas yongasu mi skyo ba dang / thos pa thams cad kyis mi ngoms pa dang / ji ltar thos
39a2(phal chen): pa la tshul bzhin du rtog pa dang / de la mngon sum du mnyam par gnog pa dang / sgro 'dogs pa'i lta ba thams cad dang bral ba dang / chos thams cad rnam par 'byed pa la mkhas pa dang / mtshan nyid kyi phyag rgya thas
39a3(phal chen): dang ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sgo nas/ lhun gyis grub par sgom shing / rnam par sgom pa dang / stob la 'jug pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la 'jug pa rgyun mi 'chang ba dang / shes rab kyi
39a4(phal chen): pha rol tu phyin pa spro kun dang ldan pas/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i sgor 'jug pas/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongasu dag par byed// 'jig rten gyi bya ba'i rgyud thams cad ston pa dang / sems can
39a5(phal chen): yongasu smin pas yongasu mi skyo ba dang / bsam pa bzhin du bya ba spod pa dang / bya ba thams cad la mngon par chags pa med pa dang / byis pa'i spyod pa dang / 'phags pa'i spyod pa bsam pa ji lta ba bzhi
39a6(phal chen): du ston pa dang / 'khor ba pa mya ngan las 'das pa nye bar ston pa dang / sbyor ba thams cad shin tu brtags pas rgyud dang / rgyan thams cad bstan pa gnas med pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi rjesu 'gro zhing rje
39a7(phal chen): 'brang ba dang / sems can thams cad sgrol ba'i spyod pas/ thabs mkhas pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongasu spyong ngo // sems can gyi khams mthar thugs par yongasu smin par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams
39a8(phal chen): mthar thug par yongasu spyad ba dang / ngo bzhin gshegs pa mthar thug par mchod pa dang / chos chags pa med pa'i mthar thug par rnam par 'tshang rgya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings kyis mthar thugs pa'i spyod pa'i/ 
39b1(phal chen): dkyil 'khor yongasu rdzogs par bya ba dang / bskal pa phyi ma'i mthar thug par rab tu gnas pa dang / sems bskyed pa'i mthar thug par stobs la 'jug pa dang / 'gro ba dang ldog pa mthar thug par mngon par 'tshang ba dang / 
39b2(phal chen): ring gi gnas kyi mthar thug par thams cad mthong ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi mthar thug pa rab tu thob par bya bas/ smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa yong su ngag par byed// bsam pa'i stobs kun nas com
39b3(phal chen): mongs pa med pa dang / lhag pa'i bsam pa'i stobs dbang du gyur cing thub pa med pa dang / snying rje chen po'i stobs skyo ba med pa dang / byams pa chen po'i stobs snyoms pa'i sbyor ba can dang / gzungs kyi stobs ngon thams
39b4(phal chen): kyi sbyor ba la bsgribs pa med pa dang / spobs pa'i stobs 'gro ba tham sa cad tshim par byed pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa'i stobs theg pa thams cad kyi rgyan byed pa dang / smon lam gyi stobs gcang mi rung ba dang / mngon
39b5(phal chen): pa shes pa'i stobs tshad med pa mngon par bsgrub pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs la mos pa dam pa'i stobs rab tu 'dzin pas/ stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yong su dag par byed / 
39b6(phal chen): 'dod chags kyi spyod pa khong du chud ba dang / zhe sdang gi spyod pa rjesu rdzogs pa dang / gti mug gi spyod pa rab tu rtogs pa dang / cha mnyam pa'i spyod pa rjesu shes pa dang / slob pa'i sems can gyi spyod pa rab tu rtogs pa dang / 
39b7(phal chen): skad cig gcig gis sems can mtha' yas pa'i spyod pa rnam par rtog pa dang / sems dang bsam pa mtha' yas pa thams cad shes par byed pa dang / chos thams cad la yang dag par ji lta ba bzhin du rtogs
39b8(phal chen): pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs kyi rjesu 'jug pa dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi sgo thams cad dang ldan pa khong du chud pas/ ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yong su dag par byed do// 
40a1(phal chen): bam po nyi shu lnga pa// de ga de ltar pha rol tu phyin pa rnams sos spyod zhing / pha rol tu phyin pa de dag yosu rdzogs par byed pa dang / pha rol gyi phyogs mi gtong ba dang / byang chub sem
40a2(phal chen): dpa'i theg pa rgyun chen po'i rgyan dang ldan pa la gnas shing sems can gyi khams ji ltar dam bcas pa bzhin du yang dag par sgrol lo// de dag dge ba'i las shin tu bsags pa ston pas ngar seng du 'gro ba'i sems can sgro'o// 
40a3(phal chen): brtsam pa chen po la gzung bas/ sems can gyi khams mi khom par 'gro ba sgrol lo// lhag mthong che bar bltabs pas/ gzugs kyi khams na 'khod pa'i sems can gyi khams sgrol lo// phra ba'i ye shes nye bar
40a4(phal chen): bslabs pas/ gzugs med pa'i khamasu skyes pa'i sems can rnams sgrol lo// zhi ba'i tshul le bar bstabs pas/ nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la mos pa'i sems can gyi khams sgrol lo// 
40a5(phal chen): stobs bcu'i rgyan chen po dang ldan pa bstan pas/ theg pa chen po la mo sa pa'i sems can gyi khams sgrol lo// de ltar na sngor la sa dang po pa'i sa la gnas pa'i tshe/ sems can ga yangs chen po nas
40a6(phal chen): lhung ba rnam pa tha dad par gyur pa ji lta ba bzhir du shes te spro sna tshogs nas gzung bar bya'o zhes sang+ge'i sgra bsgrags pa de bzhin du/ ye shes thob pa'i rnams sems can thams cad bsgral ba'i phyir rab tu zhugs pa yin no/ 
40a7(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa' ye shes de lta bu la zhugs pa ni/ rtag tu rgyun mi gcong par sangs rgyas kyi rigs dang / chos kyi rigs dang / dge 'dun gyi rigs mi gcod pa'i phyir zhugs pa yin te/ 
40a8(phal chen): nga dag byang chub kyi sems gzhan gyi sems kyi rgyud la gzhog pas/ sangs rgyas kyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ chos kyi mdzod rnam par 'grel pa/ chos kyi rigs mi gcod pa yin bstan pa'i tshul dang 'gal ba
40b1(phal chen): mi byed pas/ ngag 'dun gyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ smon lam chen po yang dag par brjod pas/ sangs rgyas kyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i tshul yang dag par sbyor bas/ chos kyi rigs mi gcod pa
40b2(phal chen): yid/ snying po thong par byed pa'i chos la brtson pas/ dge 'dun gyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa bon sems can gyi zhing la 'debs pas/ sangs rgyas kyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ dam pa'i
40b3(phal chen): chos yong su 'dzin pas/ chos kyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ tshogs chen po yongasasu sdud ba mi skyo bas/ dge 'dun gyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / nga lngar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
40b4(phal chen): rnams kyi mdzad pa dran pa'i phyir/ rtag tu de bzhin gshegs pa'i gang mas ngag dang rje su bstan pa mi gtong bas/ sangs rgyas dang / chos dang dge 'dun gyi rigs mi gcod pa yin/ de dag de ltar skyabs
40b5(phal chen): gsum gyi rigs mi gcad pa'i phyir zhugs pas rtsom pa thams cad la kha na ma tho ba med pa yin te/ brtsam pa gang ci rtsom yang rung de dag thams cad thogs pa med par thams cad mkhyen pa'i sbyor
40b6(phal chen): 'byung ba thob par byed // de dag de ltar lus kyi las kha na ma tho ba med pa dang / ngag gi las khan ma tho ba med pa dang / yid kyi las kha na ma tho ba med pa la gnas pas/ dge ba'i rtsa ba rtsom pa don yod par rtsom pa yin/ 
40b7(phal chen): sems can gyi ngor sbyor 'don yong bar rtsom mo// sems can ngor yong bar 'dul bar byed// chos don yod par ston to// de'i chos ston pa thams cad kyang sems can gyi bsam pa tshim par bya ba la thog pa med
40b8(phal chen): pas bong du chung bar 'gyur// de'i sems bskyad pa gcig tsam yang log par mi 'gyur te/ sems bskyed pa gzhan thangs dang shes rab kyi yong su zin pa thams cad kyang / thams cad mkhyen panyi du yongs sngon
41a1(phal chen): dede ltar chos dkang po bsags pa don yod pa de lta bu la gnas pas/ rgyan rnam par phye ba bcus sems bskyed pa thams cad yongasu bsngo ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar lus kyi rgyan sems ca
41a2(phal chen): 'dul ba ji bzhin du yang dag par ston pa dang / ngag gi rgyan the tsom thams cad gcod pa dang / sems kyi rgyan skad cig gcig gis ting 'dzin rjesu rtogs par byed pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rgyan kun nas nyon mongs
41a3(phal chen): pa meng ba dang / 'od kyi rgyan 'od zer gyi dra ba mtha' dang dbus med pa bkye bas/ 'gro ba thams cad snang bar byed pa dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor gyi rgyan sems can gyi rnam pa tshad med pa'i tshogs yongasu mgu bar byed
41a4(phal chen): ba dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rnam par 'phrul pa'i rgyan sems can gyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du/ rdzu 'phrul gyi rnam par 'phrul pa dang / bstan pa'i rgyan mkhas pa'i skye bo thams cad kyis yongasu gzung ba dang / mya ngan
41a5(phal chen): las 'das pa'i rgyan mngon par sangs rgyas pa gcig gis phyogs bcu ma lus par rgyas par 'gengs pa dang / chos byin gyi sa brlab pa'i rgyan yul dang dus dang / snong ji lta ba bzhin du sdong
41a6(phal chen): bdag ste/ de dag rgyan de lta dus sems bskyed pa thams cad mngon par bsgrub pas/ lus dang ngag dang / yid kyi las don yod pa dang / ye shes chen po don yod pa rab tu 'thob ste/ dedag mthong bas kyang 'ang/ 
41a7(phal chen): ltar bla na med ba yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yongasu smin par 'gyur ba'i phyir/ sems can rnams la don yod pa yin te/ thos pa dang / bsnyen bkur ba dang / 'grogs pa dang / rjesu dran pa dang / 
41a8(phal chen): rjesu rab tu byung ba dang / chos ston pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba la rjesu yid rangs pa dang / dad cing mos pa dang / chung ngu na ming brjod pa tsam yang 'di ltar bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yod su/ 
41b1(phal chen): smin pa'i phyir/ sems can rnams la don du 'gyur ba yino// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ 'di lta ste dper na/ rtsi'i ming mthong nab ba zhes bya ba de mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams kyi lus la zhen pa 'am/ ltor zos pa'i
41b2(phal chen): dug rab tu ni bar 'gyuraro// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de bzhin du chos de lta bu dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' yang mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams kyi nyon mongs pa'i dug thams cad byang bar 'gyur te/ chos dkar po'i
41b3(phal chen): stobs kyi shugs kyang skye bar 'gyuraro// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos nyid de lta bu dang ldan zhing chos de dag la gnas te/ shes rab kyi 'od chen pos ma rig pa'i rur ba
41b4(phal chen): bsal nas/ bdud kyi dkrugs ma'i 'khor thams cad byams pa dang snying rje chen po'i stobs kyis pham par byas te/ ye shes dang bsod rnams kyi stobs kyi shugs kyis phas kyi rgol ba thams cad zil
41b5(phal chen): gyis mnan nas/ rdo rje lta bu'i ting 'dzin la 'jug pas/ sems kyi dri ma thams cad dang / nyon mongs pa'i phyogs thams cad bsal nas/ skyo ba med pa'i stobs dang shugs kyi dge ba'i rtsa/ 
41b6(phal chen): ba phur sum tshogs pa thams cad rab tu sgrub ste/ sngan chang sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongasu dag par spyad pa'i stobs dang shugs kyis mi khom pa dang / ngan song dang ngan 'gro'i lam thams cad rnam par bzlog nas/ mngon par
41b7(phal chen): zhen pa med pa'i stobs dang shugs kyis/ ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor longasu sbyangs te/ rim gyi thabs dang shes rab kyi stobs dang shugs kyis byang chub sems dpa'i sa dang pha rol tu phyin pa dang / ting 'dzin dang / 
41b8(phal chen): mngon par shes pa dang / rig pa dang mi 'jigs pa yongasu dag pa mngon par bsgrubs nas/ chos dbar po thams cad kyi stobs dang shugs kyis/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi mtshan dang / dpe byang bzang po dang / 
42a1(phal chen): sru nga gsung nga thugs kyi rgyun yong su ngas pa mngon par bsgrub pa rab tu rgyas par bste/ ye shes kyis shes par bya ba'i dbang dang / byin gyis brlabs kyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stongs
42a2(phal chen): dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa thams cad ma'am pa nyid du khong du chud par byas nas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyang myur du 'thob cing / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi yul yang ston
42a3(phal chen): gyi khyad par ji lta ba bzhin du 'thob par 'gyuraro// sngon gyi byin gyi rlabs dang / ye shes kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis mngon par sangs rgyas nas/ sems can rnams kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du/ sangs rgyas kyi shing stan
42a4(phal chen): te/ 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin du sems can rnams la chos kyi lato ra lo chen po bskor cing mtha' yas pa'i sems can rnam par 'du'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' chos de lta bu dang ldan
42a5(phal chen): bdag ni/ tshul de wa bus sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam pa yid kyi bar du thong par 'gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thob nas kyang / 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' yas bdag tu
42a6(phal chen): dam pa'i chos yong su 'dzin cing chos smra ba chen po 'ang byed// de ltar chos smra ba byed pa'i tshe/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyis byin gyis brlabs pa de dag chos kyi
42a7(phal chen): mdzod chen po gzung zhing bsrung ba'i phyir/ tha dad pa yang dag par shes pas/ chos kyi chu rab tu dbye ba'i rjesu song ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i tshig gis 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor mtha' yas par/ bdag gis
42a8(phal chen): lus kyi rgyan byin gyis rlabs te bstan pa mngon par bsgrub pa rnam pa'i mchog thams cad dang ldan pa dang / tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa'i mkhas pa mtha' yas pa dang / ye shes mi zad pa'i sgor 'jug pa dang / dbyangs kyi
42b1(phal chen): dkyil 'khor shin tu rnam par phye ba'i byin gyis rlabs dang / dbyangs gcig bsgrags pas 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad mgu bar byed pa'i dbyangs kyi yan lag rnab par dag pa bsam pa dang / bag la nyal ba dang / shes
42b2(phal chen): ba'i sa ji lta ba bzhin du rjesu 'brang ba dang / lus kyi byin gyis rlabs kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi nang du phyin kyang zil gyis mi non pa dang / lus kyi rgyan sgro thams cad rnam par bstan pa dang / 'khor gyi dkyil
42b3(phal chen): 'khor thams cad kyi sems dang / bsam pa khong du chud pas/ rab tu rtogs pa dang / tshig grol ba'i byin gyis rlabs kyis bstan pa dang / chos 'chang ba'i byir gyi rlabs la mkhas pas/ chos kyi gtam chen po byed de/ 
42b4(phal chen): stongs dang shugs kyi dang thub pa med pa dang / 'jigs pa med pa'i dbang rum ba med pa dang / chos kyi dbang zil gyis mi non pa dang / ye ye/ sa kyi dbang gzhan gyis mi thub pa dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa
42b5(phal chen): dbang chos kyi mtshan nyid 'khrugs pa med pa dang / tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa'i dbang mtshams sbyor ba rgyur chang ba med par bsam pa shin tu rtogs pa dang / gzungs kyi dbang chos thams cad rnam
42b6(phal chen): par gdon mi za ba la 'jug pa dang / smon lam gyi dbang dpe sna tshogs kyis bstan pa'i tshul bye bar bsgrub pa shin tu bstan pa dang / snying rje chen po'i dbang phyir mi ldog cing rgyun ma chad pa dang / byams pa chen po'i dbang
42b7(phal chen): sngon shin tu skyes pas/ bsam pa thams cad sim par byed pa'i 'od zer gyi dra ba chen po gtong pas chos kyi gtam chen po byed// de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa seng ge'i gdan la bzhugs shing chos kyi gtam
42b8(phal chen): gsung ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' ye shes dang smon lam gyi khyad par dang ldan pa ma gtogs par sems can gyi ris na/ byang chub sems dpa' de la phyir brgal ba 'am/ spyi gtsug blta ba 'am/ zil gyis gnar ba
43a1(phal chen): 'am/ dri ba'i tshogs yongasu dri bas thub par bya bar nus pa'i sems can gang yang med/ de ni gnas medo// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ gal te byang chub sems dpa' dbang de lta bu thob pa la/ 'jig
43a2(phal chen): rten gyi khams brjod med pa tsam du yangs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor cig yod la/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor de yang sems can stong gsum gyi bdag po'i gzi brjid thob pa sha stag gis gang ba zhig yin na yang / 
43a3(phal chen): de dag thams cad byang chub sems dpa' 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du 'ongs ma thag tu lus bstan pa'i dbang gi zil gyis mnan te/ byams pa chen po'i dbang gis lus kyi gzhi tshim par byas nas/ ye shes chen po
43a4(phal chen): dbang gis sems dang bsam pa rnam par shes par bya ste/ mi 'jig sa pa'i bsam pa chen pos chos ston pa byed cing / spobs pa chen bo'i dbang gi sems can tshim par byeng// kye rgyal ba'i sras// de ci'i
43a5(phal chen): phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' de ni ye shes kyi la 'khor tshad med pa dang / chos rnam par 'byed pa shin/ tu rnam par phye ba la mkhas pa dang ldan/ dran pa'i stobs dang shug
43a6(phal chen): mnyams dashing rgya che ba dang ldan/ chos thams cad kyi tshul rnam par gdon mi za bar bzung zhing blangs pas rtogs par mkhas pa dang ldan/ byang chub sems dpa'i thabs mkhas pa mtha' dbus med pa dang ldan/ 
43a7(phal chen): chos kyi mtshar nyid bsgribs pa med pa'i chos ston pa la mkhas pa dang ldan/ mos pa la mkhas pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis blangs pa dang ldan/ dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs
43a8(phal chen): ba'i dkyil 'khor du yang dag par gzhol ba'i ye shes kyi byin gyis brlabs la mkhas pa dang ldan/ sems can thams cad gtso bo 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba rnams dang / rgyud kyi
43b1(phal chen): gcig tu gyur pa'i bsam pa bzang po rnam par dag pa la mkhas pa dang ldan pas/ chos smrab chen po byed cing / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi chos kyi mdzod kyang rnam par 'byed// 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i nga
43b2(phal chen): ba'ir gshegs pa rnams kyi ye shes kyi byin gyis brlabs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i yid kyi spon lam dang / ye shes 'byam klas pas dam pa'i chos kyang yongasu 'dzin to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi tha
43b3(phal chen): gros kyis/ yang byang chub sems dpa' rim gyis yang dag par 'byung ba'i chos sgo'i le'u yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis/ de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smraso// bsod nams
43b4(phal chen): tshogs bsags byang chub sems la gnas pa rnams// rtag tu ba g.yod blo brtan mthu chen 'dog pa dag/ dran dang ldan zhing byang chub sems rab mi gtong bas// phyogs rnams bcu bor bde gshegs rnams ni
43b5(phal chen): mnyes par byed// brtson 'grus brtsams pa dran ldan mos pa bar+Na/ na pa can// 'jig rten kun la rtag tu mi gnas mi ldog pa// zab pa'i chos zhugs mya ngan med pa'i tshul mkhas rnams// phyogs
43b6(phal chen): rnams bcur por bde gshegs rnams ni mnyes par byed// brtson 'grus bstan pas bde gshegs mnyes par byas nas kyang // dus gsum bsod nams tshogs dang ye shes ldan pa'i rnams// sa rnams ca
43b7(phal chen): byed spyod mchog nyams pa med par byed// thub pa'i smon lam rdzogs byed ston pa'ang de bzhin byed// ye shes gcig la zhugs pa de dag thob bya ba// thob nas 'gro ba kun la sbyin pa rab tu gtong // bsam pa dag
43b8(phal chen): dngang khams dang sbyor ba shes byas nas// dbang po ji bzhin mkhas pa de ltar chos kyang ston// pha rol phyin pa brtson pa mthu chen ldan pa'i rnams// 'gro ba rnams la chos ston bdag gi don mi gtong // pha rol
44a1(phal chen): phyir rdzogs grol ba mthu chen ldan pa'i rnams// khyu mchog mthu yis 'khor ba'i tsho las sems can stsol// de ltar nyin mtshan smyo ba med par brtson byed cing // drang srong rgyal na chos
44a2(phal chen): rigs mi gcong zhugs pa yis// dkar po'i spyod pa gang yang rung sa spyod pa'i rnams// thams cad don yod rgyal ba rnams kyi sar 'gro'o// de dag ci spyod thams cad 'gro ba rnams la yang // rnam smin don yod
44a3(phal chen): na mongs dri ma sbyong bar 'gyur// 'di 'dra'i chos ldan de dag mun pa bsal byas shing // bdud 'khrug 'khor lo pham byas byang chub thob par byed// de ltar brtson zhing ye shes thob pa'i bde gshegs sras// bdeg phye
44a4(phal chen): rnams kyi chos rangab mdzod kyang rab tu ston// de dag chos smra'i bya ba ku na kyang shin tu byed// bdud rtsi mchog zhim sprin gyi char yang mngo na par 'bebs// de dag snying rje byams pas 'gro ba kun bkang zhing / 
44a5(phal chen): brtan pa de rnams 'khor gyi bsam pa shes byas nas// gang gi tha/ sam pa blo gros sems rgyud ci 'dra ba// de bzhin rgyal ba'i rtsa// sa ni stong phrag dum ston// glang po'i skabs sdug tshul bzang 'gro sa
44a6(phal chen): 'gro ba'i rnams// seng ge'i rtsal ltar rtag tu sus kyang mi thub cing // ye shes rgya mtsho lta bu ri rab bzhin gnas pa// sprin+da ltar 'gro ba kun gyi nyon mongs zhi bar byed// byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi blo gros kyis
44a7(phal chen): de skad ces smras pa dang // de la ston pas rjesu dges par mdzad// shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo// sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba las/ chos snang ba'i le'u zhes bya ba ste/ nyi shu gsum pa'o// 
44a8(phal chen): de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus// shar phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad dang / lho phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad dang / gzhung de bzhin du phreng gi phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi bar thams cad
44b1(phal chen): na/ gying bzhi pa 'di la sogs pagreng bani pa re re na/ de bzhin gshegs pa mang po bzhugs par snang// byang chub sems dpa' de dag kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi rlabs kyis chos ston to// bdag bdag kyang de bzhin pa
44b2(phal chen): pa'i zhabs kyi drung na 'khod par she so// bcom ldan 'das kyis rdzu 'phrul mngon par 'du mdzad pa ma bshig ma btang bar byang chub kyi shing drung yang ma spangs par ri rab kyi rtse mo nas/ mtshe ma'i gnas kyi lha'i bu rab mtshe ma'i
44b3(phal chen): khang nga nor bu sna tshogs gang na ba der gshegs par snang// ji ltar gling ngas pa 'dzin/ bcom ldan 'das rab mtshe ma'i gan su gshegs par snang ba de bzhin du/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na yang / rab mtsha ma'i gams
44b4(phal chen): su gshegs par snang ste/ byin gyi rlabs snga ma rnams kyang de bzhin ma 'ukhrugs par snang // de nas lha'i rgyal po rab mtshems bcom ldan 'das rgyang ring po nas/ khang pa nor bu sna tshogs log su mngon par
44b5(phal chen): gshegs pa mthong nas/ rings pa'i gzugasu khang pa nor bu sna tshas kyi nang du de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdan rdzu 'phrul gyis bas+t+ra bas pa'i seng ge'i khri pad+mo'i snying po can/ lha rdzas kyi rin po che las
44b6(phal chen): byas pa/ 'og re brgya stong phrag bcus brgyan pa/ gser gyi dra ba brgya stong phrag bcus kun nas mngon par bres pa/ me tog gi bla rab rgya stong drag bcus kun tu khyab par byas pa/ phreng ba'i bla re brgya stong phrag bcu kun tu rdzus
44b7(phal chen): ba/ spos kyi bla re brgya stong phrag bcus spos thams cad kun tu 'thul par bdugs pa/ rin po che'i bla re brgya stong phrag bcus kun tu bres pa/ me thog gi gdugs brgya stong phrag bcu kun nas bzung ba phreng ba
44b8(phal chen): gsus dargya song bas bcus ku sa bzung ba/ rin po che'i gdubyas pacu stong phrag bcu 'a mas bzung ba/ 'od zer brgya stong brag bcus snang bar byas pa/ rab mama'i lha'i rgyal po brgya stong drag bcus rab tu btung pa
44'a1(phal chen): tshangs pa brgya stong drug bcus mngon par byag bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' brgya stong drag bcus mngon par bstong pa rol mo brdu ba brgya stong drag bcu'i sA byung ba chos kyi glu'i dngas brgya stong drag

44'b1(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das gshegasasu gsol/ bde bar gshegs pa gshegs gsol/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas bde bar gshegs sam/ de nas bcom ldan 'das lnga'i rgyal po rab mtshams

46a2(phal chen): 'das la phyag 'tshal nas/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus phyogs bcu rgyas par byas te/ gang nas 'ongs pa'i phyog su brtan nas/ sang+ga'i khri rin po che'i snying po can dag pa shams te/ skyil mo krung bcas nas 'khod ngo // ji ltar
46a3(phal chen): gling bzhi pa 'di'i rab ra tshe ma'i gnas byang chub sems dpa' 'ongs par gyur pa de bzhin du/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gling bzhi pa kun tu yang / rab mtshe ma'o gnas kyi khang pa/ nor bu sna tshogasu
46a4(phal chen): 'ang lhag par gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa'i ming yang de skad ces bya ba sha stag/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan kyang de skad ces bya ba'i ba 'bring na tshangs par spyod pa sha sta go// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs
46a5(phal chen): kyi bol gnyis nas/ 'od zer bye ba brgya stong bkye ste/ phyogs pa cu thams cad snang bar byas nas/ 'jig rten gyi khamasaHmas cad bstan te/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag gis/ 'jig rten
46a6(phal chen): gyi khams thams cad kyi gling ba ni ba kun gyi rang mtshe ma'i gnas thams cad na yang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa yod pa mthong // de nas byang chub sems dpa' yon tan dang ldan pas/ sangs rgyas kyi
46a7(phal chen): mthus phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigasu bcang ba 'di dag smra so// sangs rgyas 'od zer 'od snang bas// phyogs rnams thams cad rnam par snang // des ni rab tu gsal byas pas// mig la rab rig
46a8(phal chen): gang yang med// mtshe ma rab kyi gnas 'jim/ gang zag dam pa sangs rgyas bzhugs// de bzhin kur na 'ang gsal bar snang // de ni 'jig rten ngo mtshar to// sems can gtso bo bcu'i rnams// gshegs par
46b1(phal chen): gyur bas mngon par bstod// de dag 'khor kyang ci 'dra ba// de bzhin du kur rag tu snang // phyogs rnams bcu po thams cad na// chos kyi ngas pa rab tu stod// de kun ming yang de bzhin te// bdag cag rnams kyi ku rdzo
46b2(phal chen): bzhim 'jig rten khams kyi ming dag kyang // de zhes bya ba kun nas 'ongs// gang zag dab pa de dag ni// tshangs pa'i spyod pa'ang den spyod// bdag cag rnams la gang btags pa// kun gyi ming yang de dang 'thun/ 
46b3(phal chen): sangs rgyas zhing rnams 'thun ldan pa// de dag sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul pa'o// mi'i 'jig rten kun na'ang // 'di na rgyal ba bzhugs par shes// gzhan gyis de'i rgyal po yi// gnas na de bzhin bzhugs pa mthong
46b4(phal chen): po/ 'jig rten khams rnams thams cad na// gang zag ngas pa de bzugs kyang // rgyal ba mtshos rab gnas na// bzhugs par bangag cag kun kyang sems// 'jig rten khams rnams thams cadam/ 
46b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas gzi brjing bsam mi khyad// de dag smor lam bsru ba'i phyir// 'jig rter kham su rab tu bkye// sems can gtso bo'i rnam 'phrul pa// 'di dag de rnams kun gyis mthong / sas
46b6(phal chen): yon tan mtha' yas te// 'jig rten zang zing thub pas spangs// phyogs rnams thams cad kun tu rgyu// chags pa med pa na mkha' bzhin// de ni gcig las shin tu 'das// mang po dag tu'ang mi dmigaso// mtha'
46b7(phal chen): yas legs mnga' sangs rgyas rnams// de dag shes par ji ltar rung // gnas pa med cing len pa meng // chos dbyings rtogs par thugasu chung // de nas byang chub sems dpa' blo gros dang ldan pas// sangs rgyas
46b8(phal chen): kyi byin gyis rlangs kyis// phyogs bcur rnam par bltas ste// de'i mi tshig su bcad pa 'di dag sbaso// 'jig rten mngon po 'phrul chen rnams// rdul mo gang zag ngas pa dam/ 'dus shing tshogs pa bsam sas pa'i
47a1(phal chen): bskal bdag tu shi tu shes// de ga thams cad kun gzigs pa// sems canag tsa bo'ang mdzad// srog chags kun la phan pa'i phyir// sems can rnams la chos son to// 'jig
47a2(phal chen): run nag 'di dag tu// 'jig rten mgon po byung gyur pa// 'jig rter sgror ma de dag ni// blta bar shin tu dka' ba yin// sbyin pa tshul khrims bzod pa'i rab// brtson 'grus bsam gtan bsgom pa dang / shes rab sngan
47a3(phal chen): chang spyad pas na// 'gro ba thams cad snang bar mdzad// sangs rgyas 'dra ba gang yang med// de phyir de dang mnyam pa med// chos rnams yod pa ma yin pas// skyes bu'i dam pa mthong ba med// sangs rgyas shes rab chen
47a4(phal chen): po rnams// mtshan gyi tshogs ni bsam mi khyab// sku'i tshogs kyis shim tu 'phags// chos rnams kun gyis yang dag byung // 'jig rjen grags chen dag pa'i rnams// dpa' ba chen po de dag snang // de dag
47a5(phal chen): mtshan tsam thos pas kyang // ngan song thams cad spadras par 'gyu ra// bskal pa rnams ni brjod med par// byang chub don dur/ khor byas kyang // 'di'i tshul ni ma shes na// byang chub don du zhugs
47a6(phal chen): pa min// sangs rgyas bsam gyis mi khyab pa// bskal pa bye bar bkur ba dang // gang gis tshul 'di bsam pa gnyis// 'di ni de las khyad 'phags// gang gis brjod yas zhing gi rnams// rin chen gang ste thub
47a7(phal chen): gsol kyang // 'di'i tshul ni ma shes na// sangs rgyas byang chub de la ring // de nas byang chub sems dpa' dpal dang ldan pas// sangs rgyas kyis byin gyi rlabs kyis// phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te// de'i tshe
47a8(phal chen): tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smra so// namakha' dri ma med pa la// nyi ma'i 'od zer mtha' yas pa// dpyid kyi zla ba tha ma la// phyogs bcu dag tu rab tu snang // de tshe smig rgyu ci 'dra ba// de dag bgrang bar mi nus te/ mig
47b1(phal chen): can rnams kyang de la rmongs// long ba rnams kyi spyod yul min// de bzhin sems can gtso bo yi// yon tan mtha' dang dbus med pa// bskal pa bsam gyis mi khyab par// sus kyang shes par mi nuso// de dag gang nas
47b2(phal chen): blangs pa med// de bzhin sus kyang byas pa med// de ni ci las skyes pa med// rnam par bsgoms na yod pa min// 'ongs pa med pa'i chos rnams la// 'gro ba de bzhin mi dmigs te// de phyir de dag rgyu yang med// de bzhin
47b3(phal chen): 'jig pa'ang yong ba ming// 'jig pa med pa'i chos rnams kyi// rang bzhin gang gis shes pa ni// gang la skye ba med pa yi// yang dag sangs rgyas mthong ba min// skyes pa med pa'i chos rnams kyi// rang bzhin dngos
47b4(phal chen): bo mi dmigs te// de 'dri'i don du shes pas ni// dmigs pa med pa tshas 'di la shes byed gang yang med// chos rnams thams cad mam na cing med// chos 'di 'di ni shes gyur na// yongasu shes pa gang yang
47b5(phal chen): med skye ba dag ni brjod pa ste// de phyir zhing rnams rab tu brjod// ming gi rang bzhin shes gyur na// 'khrug pa med pa rab/ shes// gang tshe 'jig rten ming yin par// tshul bzhin du 'i rtog
47b6(phal chen): byed na// de tshe thams cad don bstan pa// byang chub sems dngas rab tu shes// de nas byang chub sems dpa' dga' ba dang ldan pas/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus phyogs bcur rnam par bltas ste// de'i tshe tshig su bcad
47b7(phal chen): pa 'di dag smraso// gnas 'di shin tu rgya che ste// chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa yi mo// rtag tu kun tu song ba ste// yidu 'ong zhing gnas kyang meng // de la yang dag bdag byas shing // rim gro yong par dang byed na/ 
47b8(phal chen): sdug bsngal nam yang mi mthong ste// ngan song rnams kyang mi mthong ngo // tshang med de bzhin grangs med pa'i// 'jig rten khamasu su 'gro bas// gang rnams 'din snang ba yi// sangs rgyas byin rlabs thos par 'gyur/ 
48a1(phal chen): drang srong chen po'i byin gyi rlabs// gang gis thos par gyur nas kyang // 'di 'dra sangs rgyas cho so zhes// rtog med bla med byang chub// gang rnams 'das pa'i sangs rgyas kyis// chos nyid la ni
48a2(phal chen): yid ces pa// de kun 'jig rten sgron ma ste// rkang gnyis ldan pa'i dam par 'gyur// sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul pa 'di// la la zhig gis thos gyur cing // thos nas dang par byed 'gyur na// de dag mi'i dam par
48a3(phal chen): 'gyur/ brtan pa gang rnams da ltar yang // sangs rgyas chos la dang byed pa// de dag don gzigs mi 'jigs pa'i// de bzhin gshegs par 'gyur ba yin// bskal pa bsam gyis mi khyab par// 'di 'dra thos
48a4(phal chen): pa shin tu dkon// smon lam dbang ni ma gtogs par// blo gros 'di 'drar 'gyur ba min// sangs rgyas dam chos 'di las kyang // legs par bshad pa bzung byas shing // gzhan la ston par su byed pa// 
48a5(phal chen): de dag bsam gyis mi khyab 'gyur// de la brtson 'grus bsgre/ dbyas shing // yid la go cha bgo byas te// gang las sa / ngas rgyas brjod pa yi// shes pa 'di 'dra mnyan par bya// de nas byang
48a6(phal chen): chub sems dpa' 'khrel dang ldan pas/ sangs rgyas kyis byin gyi rlobs kyis/ phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te// de'i tshe tshig su bcod smras pa/ gang zhig thos nas 'di 'dra ba'i// dga' ba yangs pa skye ba dang / 
48a7(phal chen): the tsom rnam par 'chang ba ni// 'jig rten na ni ngo mtshar che// 'di ltar thams cad gzigs pa'i rnams// nyid kyis 'gro la bka' stsal na// sangs rgyas mi mkhyen gang yang med// de ltar sangs rgyas bsam
48a8(phal chen): mi khyab// mi shes pa yi rgyu las ni// ye shes 'jug par mi 'gyur te// mun pa'i mthu dang snang ba gnyis// lhan cig 'byung ba mi 'gyur bstan// ji ltar gzugs dang gzugs med pa// bskal pa ma
48b1(phal chen): pa meng par bshad // de ltar shes dang mi shes pa// 'grogs par shing tu mi 'gyuraro// 'khor dang mya ngan 'das pa dag/ ji ltar med las btags pa ltar // de bzhin shes dang mi shes pa// mtsham cing bzhin dung migs
48b2(phal chen): ba med// ji ltar 'jig rten 'jig pa dang // 'du bar 'gyur ba ring ba ste// phan tshun 'grogs par mi 'gyur ba// shes dang mi shes de bzhino// ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' yi// thog ma'i sems dang tha ma'i sem
48b3(phal chen): ldan cig mi gnas byung ba ltar// shes dang mi shes de bzhino// ji ltar lus dang rnam shes pa// gzhan dang gzhan las 'byung 'gyur ba// de bzhin shes dang mi shes gnyis// 'grogs par 'gyur ba nam yang
48b4(phal chen): med// ji ltar drug la phan pa'i rtsi// 'phral du dug ni drug min byed// de ltar shes pa mi shes pa// shin tu sel ba byed par brjod// sangs rgyas blan gang yang med// de dang 'dra ba'ang yod pa min// de las
48b5(phal chen): gzhan du 'gyur ba med// de bas rgyal ba shin tu dgon// de nas byang chub sems dpa' brtson 'grus dang ldan pas// sangs rgya sa kyi mthus/ phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigasu bcing smras
48b6(phal chen): pa/ chos rnams 'di dag 'gal meng par// mkhyen nas sangs rgyas thug su chung // des ni mi mkhyen gang yang med// ye shes kyi 'ang pha rol phyin// ji ltar gser dang sa le sbram// ngo bo nyid kyis 'gal ba med/ 
48b7(phal chen): de ltar chos min de bzhin chos// de dag thams cad mtshan nying gcig/ sems can sems can ma yin pa// ngo bo nyid kyi rang bzhin med// gangag su med las byung ba ltar// chos rnams rang bzhin de bzhin/ 
48b8(phal chen): ma 'ongs dus ni ji lta bur// 'das pas brjod par bya ba ste// de la mtshan zhing yod pa min// de bzhin chos la mtshan yid med// 'brel par skye dang 'gog pa dang // rang bzhin med dang rang bzhin dag
49a1(phal chen): rnam pa tha dang gyur pa ltar// sangs rgyas rang bzhin de bzhi'o// mya ngan 'das pa gzung med pa// gnyis kyi dus na brjod par byas// de la bye brag gang yang med// de bzhin gzugs la rnams
49a2(phal chen): rtog pa'o// ji ltar ji zhig bgrang byas shing // bgrang bar byed ces brjod pa'ang // de la tha dad gang yang med// de bzhin gzugs kyi rang bzhin// ji ltar gcig nas gcig gi blar// mang po'i tshul du bgrang ba
49a3(phal chen): yis// dngos po grangs med 'gyur ba'ang // blo'i rnam pa tha dad bstan// 'jig rten khams rnams la la dag/ bsam gyis mi khyab tshig gyur kyang // namakha' 'jig par 'gyur ba med// rang 'byung ye shes
49a4(phal chen): de bzhin// ji ltar 'jig rten phyogs bcu yi// nam mkha' so so ru brtag pa ltar// de bzhin sangs rgyas rnam mthong ste// sangs rgyas rnams la rtog mi mnga'// de nas byang chub sems dpa' stobs
49a5(phal chen): dang ldan pas// sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ phyogs bcu rnam par/ bltas te/ de'i tshe tshig su bcad smras pa/ ji ltar dus rnam/ sa gsum po yis// sems can khams rnams brjod par gyur/ 
49a6(phal chen): sems can de dag thams cad kyang // phung po lnga las shin tu brjod// de rnams las kyi phung chen yin// las kyi rtsa ba'ang sems yin te// sems ni sgyu ma bzhin du bshang // sgyu mar gyur pa 'gro 'di
49a7(phal chen): gang na 'jig rten 'di 'byung zhing // yang na ldog par 'gyur ba yi// 'jig rten 'jig rten mi byed de// gzhan gyi rgyud kyang byas pa min// 'jig rten 'di na 'byung ba 'byung // 'jig rten 'dir yang
49a8(phal chen): ldog par 'gyur// 'byung zhes brjod par mi bya ste// de ni 'jig rten zhes pa yin// gang la 'jig rten snang ba zhes// 'du shes rnam par brtags pa yi// 'jig rten zhes bya gang zhig yin// sna ba zhes
49b1(phal chen): 'ang ci zhig nyid// dusu gsung ngas rtsu ma// drang po 'dzin 'jig rten yin// de dag 'gog pa snang ba zhes// 'gro ba dag tu 'du shes kyang // phung ba zhes bya ba 'dzi na // drang po'i rang bzhin jis bu// drang rol
49b2(phal chen): ni mi 'jig phyir// dngos po med ces rab tu brjod// phung po 'jidag rnam brtags dor// de dag rang bzhin stong pa yin// mi 'jig dor ri stong pa ste// dngos po med ces bya ba'o// 'jig rten ci bzhin sangs rgyas te/ 
49b3(phal chen): sangs rgyas chos kyang sangs rgyas rnams// ngo bo nyid kyi rang bzhin med// ma nor yang dag ji bzhin pa'i// chos nyid 'di ni rtogs gyur nas// kun gzigs thams cad mkhyen pa yi// sangs rgyas kun na rab tu snang / 
49b4(phal chen): de nas byang chub sems dpa' reg pa dang ldan pas/ sangs rgyas kyi sathas/ phyogs bcung rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshig su bci sa rab/ rang bzhin dngos po med pa yi// 'jig rten khams rnams thams
49b5(phal chen): cad kyi// sa'i khams rnams ci bzhin te// sangs rgyas rnam la phrul ngos ra che// de'i rang bzhin 'di yin la// brjod cing bsngags pa mtha' yas te// 'das pa'i 'jig rten khams rnams/ 
49b6(phal chen): sus kyang brjod pa ma yin// gzhan du sems can las kyis na// shin tu bstan par brjod pa ste// sems can rnams ni ma gtogs par// las shes bya ba ci mi dmigs// de bzhin stong pa'i las kyis kyang / 
49b7(phal chen): brjod pa rnams ni tshad med pas// sems can kun gyi lus su gyur// de la 'ongs pa gang yang med// ji ltar kha dog dbyibs kyi rnams// las kyi rgyu ni bsam mi khyab// snang yang de dag de na med// rnam par rig pa'i dngos nyid
49b8(phal chen): 'dra de bzhin sems can gtso bo yi// sku ni bsam gyis mi khyab pa// brjod pa rnams kyang tshad med par// zhing rnams kun na rab tu snang // skus ni rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas min// sangs rgyas rnams la sku mi mnga'/ 
50a1(phal chen): dpa' bo chen po chos sku ste// chos ku rtoms par grug du rung // gang gisa'ang 'byung rnams kyi sku/ yang 'ardzi ba'i mjeng ba'i// sangs rgyas chos ni rnam ku dang / chos rnams la'ang rmongs pa med/ 
50a2(phal chen): 'das par gyur pa'i chos rnams kun// mya ngan 'das par shes gyur na// de dag shin tu mi gnas pa'i// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mthong ba yin// yang dag sangs rgyas sus mthong zhing // dran pa shin tu bsgom byas te/ 
50a3(phal chen): mtshan med tha dad med pa'i rnams// de dag chos kyi rgyal po'i sras// de nas byang chub sems dpa' blo dang ldan pas// sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i cha tshig su bcing smras pa// ji lta
50a4(phal chen): ri mo'i las rnams la// tshon rnams sna tshogs kun 'dug// kun kyang 'byung ba chen por ma'am// sems kyis yongs brtags pa yin// khams la tshon rtsing ngag med// tshon rtsi la'ang khams med de// khamra
50a5(phal chen): rnams ma gtogs gzhanan yang // tshon ces bya ba gang yang med sems la ri mo de med de// ri mo la'ang sems medo// sem/ sa de ma gtogs gzhin du'ang // ri mo gang yang mi dmig so// sem
50a6(phal chen): de rtag pa ma yin pa// bsam gyis mi khyab tshad med cing // phan tshun shes pa med pa yi// gzugs rnams thams cad ston par byed// ji ltar ri mo mkhan gyi rnams// sems ni gang gis ri me // bris pa'i
50a7(phal chen): sems kyang mi shes pa// de bzhin chos kyi rang bzhi no// sems ni ri mo mkhan dang 'dra// sems ni phung po byed pa ste// 'jig rten khams na ji snyed pa'i// 'jig rten 'di dag sems kyis bris// sems dang 'dra ba
50a8(phal chen): sangs rgyas te// sangs rgyas ji bzhin 'gro ba'o// sems dang sangs rgyas dag la yang // ngo bo nyid kyis zang ba med// sems kyi rgyud rnams ci 'dra ba// de dag sangs rgyas rab tu mkhyer// de phyir sangs rgyas
50b1(phal chen): rang bzhin gyis// 'gro ba sna tshogs gyur par snang // lus kyi rnams la sems med de// sems la'ang lus rnams yod pa min// sangs rgyas mdzad pa'ang rab tu byed// de ltar spyod pa ngo mtshar che// gang zhig dus gsu
50b2(phal chen): thams cad kyi// rgyal ba thams cad shes 'dod na// sangs rgyas thams cad sems kyi dngos// chos kyi dbyingasu blta bar gyis// de nas byang chub sems dpa' ye shes dang ldan pas/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ phyogs
50b3(phal chen): bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigasu bcang smras pa/ gzung du med la 'dzin ces bya// snang ba med pa snang ba ste// mnyan du med par ldan par byed// sems med pa'i sems dang ldan// tshad med pa la chang ma yis// 
50b4(phal chen): gang zhig 'dzin par mi 'dod pa// de ni tshad pad tshang ma yis// nam yang 'dzin par mi 'gyur ro// brjod med pa smra byed pa// bdag la shin tu slu ba ste// de'i dor kyang rdzogs mi byed/ srog chags
50b5(phal chen): rnams kyang tshim mi 'gyur// de ba'i na mtha' yas brjod ldan 'i// brjod pa gang zhig smra 'dong ba// bskal pa grangs med tha sa byas kyang // rang 'byung rnams kyi brjod mi zang // yid bzhin nor bu
50b6(phal chen): dag pa ni// kha dag kun tu rab tu snang // de la kha dog yod pa min// sangs rgyas yon tan de bzhin// ji ltar na mkha' dri med cing // gzugs med bstan du med yin yang // gzugs rnams thams cad ston par byed/ 
50b7(phal chen): rab kha' snang ba gang yang med// de bzhin thams cad gzigs pa'i rnams// yon tan kun dang ldan ston kyang // de ni sus kyang mthong ba med// sems la'ang de ni mi gnaso// sangs rgyas sgra ni grags mod kyi// de bzhin
50b8(phal chen): gshegs pa sna ma yin// sgra ni ma gtogs gzhan du'ang // sangs rgyas shes par mi rung // ji ltar bdag gis mthong tshul du// 'di ri shes bya'i gnas ma yin// sangs rgyas byang chub blang
51a1(phal chen): du med// de la rnam par rtog pa med// sangs rgyas chos rnams gang dag kyang // su la'ang sangs rgyas gsung ba med// sems can bsam pa ji bzhin du// de la de 'dra ston pa mdzad// 
51a2(phal chen): shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo// sangs rgyas pal po che zhes bya ba las// rab mtshe ma'i gnasu/ byang chub sems dpa' 'dus pas/ tshogasu bcang pa bstan pa'i le'u shes bya ba ste/ li shu lnga pa'o// 
51a3(phal chen): bam pa nyi ga drug pa/ de nas de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' yon tan dang ldan pas/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ byang chub sems dpa'i ting 'dzin shin tu rnam bye ba'i rnam par 'byeng ba zhes bya ba la ma
51a4(phal chen): par bzhag par gyur to// de ltar byang chub sems dpa' yon tan pa ldan pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i ting 'dzin rnam par bye ba'i rnam par 'byed pa de la mnyam par bzhag ma thag tu/ de'i tshe phyogs bcur
51a5(phal chen): rer yang 'jig rten gyi khams/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing stong phrag/ bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'das pa'i pha rol nas/ de bzhi/ na gshegs pa'i mtshan yon tan dang ldan pa zhes bya ba// sangs
51a6(phal chen): rgyas kyi zhing stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra basbed kyis zhal bstan po mthong ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis de la 'di snyed ces bka' stsal to// yon tan dang ldan pa de ltar khyod byang chub
51a7(phal chen): sems dpa'i ting 'dzin shin tu rnam par bye ba'i rnam par 'byed pa la mnyam par bzhag pa leg so leg so// rigs kyi bu khyod la ni de bzhin gshegs pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra
51a8(phal chen): ba sbed thams cad kyang mtshan 'thun pa sha stag gis/ 'di ltar bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyi sngon gyi smon lam dang / sngon gyi byin gyi rlabs dang / byang chub sems dpa'
51b1(phal chen): rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsabs shin tu brtan pas na/ 'di ltar chos bstan pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi ye shes rnam par 'phel bar bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams la 'jug par bya ba dang / sems can gyi khas rnam par bsgom
51b2(phal chen): pa dang / chags pa med pa la 'jug par bya ba dang / sgribs pa med pa'i spyod yul dang / kun nas rab tu sbyor ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa rab tu bsgrub pa dang / chos thams cad khong du chud par bya ba dang / dbang po thad
51b3(phal chen): yongasu shes par bya ba dang / chos bstan pa thams cad yongasu gzung bar bya ba dang / 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bcu 'artsam pa rab tu 'thob bar bya ba'i phyir/ byin gyi brlab pa mdzad kyis/ rigs kyi bu khyod
51b4(phal chen): kyis sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis chos 'di bstan pa la spobs par gyis shig/ de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis/ byang chub sems dpa' yon tan
51b5(phal chen): dang ldan pa la chags pa med pa nyid le bar bsgrub pa mdzad / @sgribs pa med pa nyid le bar bsgrub pa mdzad// byin gyi rlabs nyid nye bar bsgrub pa mdza // slob dpor med pa zhing se bar
51b6(phal chen): bsgrub pa mdzad// rmongs pa med pa nyid le bar bsgrub pa mdzad// tha dad pa med pa ying le bar bsgrub pa mdzad // kha na ma tho ba med pa 'i dge bar bsgrub pa mdzod // tshad med pa ling so bar bsgrub pa mdza// 
51b7(phal chen): zil gyi mi non pa yid le bar bsgrub pa mdzad // zhum pa med pa yid le bar bsgrub pa mdzad // rdo bo'i phyir zhe na/ ting 'dzin 'di yid kyi chos shing thob pa'i phyiraro// de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag
51b8(phal chen): gis phyag g.yas pa brkyang ste/ byang chub sems dpa' yon tan dang ldan pa'i mgo la byug pa mdza // sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis de ltar reg ma thag tu/ byang chub sems dpa' yon na
52a1(phal chen): / dang ldan pa/ ting 'dzin de las langs te/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams la spras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa'i las ni bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ de ni 'di ltar chos
52a2(phal chen): kyi dbyings kyis kla so// mamakha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams ni/ 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
52a3(phal chen): rnams kyi spyod pa la'ang slo'o// ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi spyod ba la'ang slob bo// nga ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi spyod pa la'ang slob bo// kye rgyal ba'i sras ngas/ 
52a4(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa gang la bsams te/ de skad du smras pa de dog gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag bcu po 'dir ga ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa/ sangs rgyas
52a5(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung / rnams kyis gsung ba dang / gsung ba dang / gsung bar 'gyu rab ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ dga' bar byed pa zhes
52a6(phal chen): bye ba byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang po dang / bde ba bskyed pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa gnyis pa dang mi mthun pa des bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa gsum pa dang / mi zad pa zhes bya ba byang
52a7(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bzhi pa dang / rmongs pa med pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa lnga pa dang / lta ba bzang po zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa drug pa dang / gnas med pa zhes bya ba byang chub
52a8(phal chen): sems dpa'i spyod pa bdun pa dang / thub par ga' ba zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa brkyang dang / chos bzang po zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dgu pa dang / bded pa dang ldan pa zhes bya ba byang
52b1(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bcu bdag ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba rnams kyis
52b2(phal chen): gsungs pa dang / gsung ba dang / gsung bar 'gyur ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de la byang chub sems dpa'i spyong ba dang po dga' bar byed pa zhes bya ba gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag 'di la byang chub sems
52b3(phal chen): dpa' sems dpa' chen po/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sngon gyi spyod pa'i rjes slob cing // rjesu dran par bya ba dang / ying zhum pa med pa dang / yid dang bas kun tu 'brel bar bya ba dang / yongasu bzung ba dang / 
52b4(phal chen): yang dag par bstad pa dang / rjes rgya che bar byed cing / sdug bsngal ba'i sems can bde bar bya ba'i phyir/ sems can thams cad la bdog pa thams cad yongasu gtong ba dang / 'gyod pa med pa'i sems kyi sbyor ba dang / 
52b5(phal chen): rnam par smin pa la ye brngam pa med pa dang / grags pa 'dod pa med pa dang / gzhan 'dod pa med pa dang / khe 'dod pa med pa dang // gzhan rjesu bsrung ba dang / pha rol la phan gdags pa dang / 
52b6(phal chen): sems can thams cad la phan gdags pa'i sems kyis/ sbyin pa'i bdag po sbyin pa byed pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag 'di ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang po'o// spyod pa de la gnas pa'i byang chub
52b7(phal chen): sems dpa' ni/ skye bo mang po'i yo'u 'ong ba yin te/ de ni sems can dbul po gang dang gang na yod pa de dang der/ smon laM gyi dbang gis rab tu skyes te/ skyes nas kyang zad mi shes pa'i long spyod dang ldan zhing / 
52b8(phal chen): shin tu drug pa yin te/ de la gal te dus gcig tu slong ba'i srog chags bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa zhig 'ongs te/ 'di skad/ kye shes par gyis shig/ bdag cag thams cad ni bkres pas
53a1(phal chen): 'chi'o// gal te bdag cag gis/ khyod kyis sha zos na ni 'tsho bar 'gyuraro// zhes tshig tu smra bar gyur kyang / byang chub sems dpa' di sbyin pa phun sum tshogs pa rnam pa 'di lta bu dang
53a2(phal chen): ldan te/ slong ba'i srog chags bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa de snyed cig le bar lhags kyang / byang chub sems dpa' la de'i phyir sems bskyed ba cig kyang zhus pa'i bsam par mi 'gyur gyi/ sems can
53a3(phal chen): de dag thams cad la/ snying rje chen po rab tu skyes te/ gzhan mang po zhig 'ongs kyang de bas kyang ches dga' ba dang / spro ba 'byung zhing 'di ltar bdag gis gsol ba ma btab par/ sangs rgyas kyi chos la yang dag par
53a4(phal chen): spobs pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen sdug bsngal zhing / slong ba sbyin pa rdzi gan su gyur pa 'di lta bu dag dang 'grogs par gyur pa ni/ bdag gis thob pa legs par thob ste/ ci nas kyang / sems can 'ag
53a5(phal chen): yid kyang mi mnyams par bya ba de ltar bdag gis bya'o// bdag gis/ dge ba'i rtsa ba ci byas pa dang / ci byed pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba ci// byed par ma gyur pa des/ ji tsam gyis sems can de dag thams
53a6(phal chen): cad 'grangs shing ngus byed par 'gyur ba de tsam du che ba'i lus su gyur cig/ sems can de dag 'grangs shing tshim par ma gyur gyi bar du gcad cing bskyabs mi zad pa de tsam gyi lus su gyur cig/ dge ba'i rtsa ba des
53a7(phal chen): kyang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par bsgrubs te/ phung po ma lus pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i khamasu mya ngan las 'das par bya'o// rnam grangs 'di bzhin du/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus kyi
53a8(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi sems can de dag thams cad las 'di 'dra ba dang ldan par gyur te/ de dag thams cad kyang bdag gi sha la zos nas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu
53b1(phal chen): yang dag par bsgrubs te/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad mnyam pa'i ye shes kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa byas nas/ phung po'i lhag ma ma lus pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings mya ngan las 'da' bar gyur cig / bang/ 
53b2(phal chen): yid kyang sems can gyi bsam pa yong su rdzogs par ma byas kyi bar dubyadag tu 'du shes pa 'am/ sems can du 'du shes pa 'am/ srid pa 'du shes pa dang / srog tu 'du shes pa 'am/ so so'i skye bor 'du shes pa 'am/ gang
53b3(phal chen): zag tu 'du shes pa 'am/ shed can du 'du shes pa 'am/ shed bdag tu 'du shes pa 'am/ byed pa por 'du shes pa 'am/ tshor ba por 'du shes pa 'am/ gzhan du chos kyi dbyings le bar gzung ba dang / sems can gyi kham
53b4(phal chen): mtha' yas pa'i chos nyid le bar gzung ba dang / stong pa'i chos kyi dbye bar gzung ba dang / 'dod chags dang bral ba'i chos ling le bar gzung ba dang / mtshan nyid med pa'i chos kyi dge bar gzung ba dang / dngos po
53b5(phal chen): med pa'i chos nyid nye bar gzung ba dang / gnas med pa'i chos nyid nye bar gzung ba dang / gzhi med pa'i chos nying le bar gzung ba dang / mngon par 'du bya ba med pa'i chos nyid nye bar gzung ba ma
53b6(phal chen): gtogs par mngon par 'tshang rgya bar ma gyur cig ces te/ de ni bdag kyang yang dag par rjesu mi mthong / bdag gi lus kyang yang dag par rje su mi mthong / len to zhes bya bar yang yang dag par rjesu mi mthong / len
53b7(phal chen): pa yang yang dag par rjesu mi mthong / sbyin pa'i gnas kyang yang dag par rjesu mi mthong ste/ de ni las kyang yang dag par rjesu mi mthong / rnam par smin pa yang yang dag par rjesu mi mthong / 'bras bu'ang yang dag par
53b8(phal chen): rjesu mi mthong / 'bras bu chen po yang dag par rjes mi mthong / 'bras bu chung yang yang dag par rje su mi mthong / de 'das pa'i dus kyi sems can thams cad kyi lus zhig pa yid la byed do// ma 'os
54a1(phal chen): pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sems can thams cad kyi lus 'jig pa yid la byeng // de 'di snyam du sems te/ kye ma/ sems can 'di dag rang gi lus grangs med pa zhig ni 'gags te/ 'gags
54a2(phal chen): cing 'gags par 'gyur yang / snying po med pa'i lus las sring po mi len pa ni ngo mtshar che'o// de lta yin gyi/ bdag gis sems can thams cad bde bas rim gro bya ba'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rjesu bslab par
54a3(phal chen): bya'o// thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyang mngon par sangs rgyas te chos thams cad rnam par sbyang ba'i phyir/ chos nyid mi 'jig pa le bar bzung ste/ dus gsum mnyam pa nyi du 'thun pa'i tshul gyis zhi bar
54a4(phal chen): bya bas sems can rnams la chos bstan par bya'o snyam du sems rdze/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dadang po ste dga' bar byed pa zhes bya'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ byang
54a5(phal chen): chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa gnyis pa bde ba skyed pa na/ bya ba de gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin te/ de ni mi gnas pa yin/ 
54a6(phal chen): gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg la mi gnas pa ston pa yin/ rigs kyi bu bdag nyid che ba la mi gnas pa yin/ rgyud kyi bdag nyid che la mi gnas pa yin/ zas kyi bdag nyid che ba la mi gnas pa yin/ gzugs kyi
54a7(phal chen): bdag nyid che ba la mi gnas pa yin/ long spyod kyi bdag nyid che ba la mi gnas pa yin te/ de ltar de ni tshul khrims las yong su nyams pa med cing / 'di ltar kun nas 'khor ba med pa dang / kun tu btsal ba med
54a8(phal chen): pa dang / yongasu gdung ba med pa dang / bar chad med pa dang / gtse ba med pa dang / 'khrul pa med par bya'o// snang ba med par bya'o// sangs rgyas kyis bsngags pa'i chos rnams yongasu gzung snyam du sems te/ 
54b1(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ byang chub sems dpa' de lta bu'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa'i drung du/ gal te yin cig tu/ bdud bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong zhig 'ongs te/ bdud re re zhing yang lha'i bu mo bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong
54b2(phal chen): 'dod pa'i cho ga thams cad la mkhas pa/ bde bar rim gror bya ba thams cad thogs pa/ lus kyi rgyan gyis lus yongasu rgyas pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong re re bstan kyang / byang chub sems dpas 'dod pa ni/ bla na

54b4(phal chen): mkhyen pa cing yid la bya ba dang mi 'dra'o// 'dod pa'i don du sem sa man 'ga' la'ang sdug bsngal gyi rgyur 'gyur bar mi byed// chung ngun srog gi dbang po 'gags par gyur kyang // gzhan la mi dga' ba na/

54b6(phal chen): lta smos kyang ci dgos te/ 'di ni gnas mdo// byang chub sems dpa' ni 'di ltar sems skyes te/ sems can 'di dag ni/ yun ring po nas de ltar gzhol ba/ de ltar 'bab pa/ de ltar bab pa/ de ltar mos pa

55a2(phal chen): te/ mi bya ba thams cad yongasu spangs pa dang / lus kyis mi shes pa thams cad yongasu spang ba ma yin pa dang / sems kyis kyang ma yin pa de ni/ bdag cag gi las yin gyis/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bdag cag gis/

62a6(phal chen): bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu don yod par 'gyuraro// dmigs pa gang gis kyang rung ste/ byang chub sems dpa' de dang 'grogs pa thams cad bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu ngon

62a8(phal chen): meng pa zhes bya ba gang zhem/ kyi rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di la byang chub sems dab tiganas med pa'i sems kyis 'jig rtem gyi khams grangs med pa la 'jug pa yin/ sengs bskyeng ba res ring grangs med pa yo
62b1(phal chen): spyo ste/ ngal gangs mi bskyed ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das grangs med pa bal ba'i phyir 'gro zhing / me tog grangs med pa dang / spos grangs med pa dang / phreng ba grangs med pa dang / drug bgrangs med pa dang / byes
62b2(phal chen): grangs med pa dang / ma bza' grangs med pa dang / ring po che grangs med pa dang / rgyal mtshan grangs med pa dang / ba dan grangs med pa dang / rgyan grangs med pa dang / mngon par 'du bya ba grangs med pas/ mngon par 'du bya ba med

62b4(phal chen): dkur ba'i don du 'gro zhing / sems bskyed pa re re la/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das grangs med pa mthong yang / sangs rgyas de dag la ga nas mi skyed pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnams la gnas mi skyed pa yin
62b5(phal chen): mtshan ma rnams la gnas mi skye ba yin/ dpe byang bzang po rnams la gnas mi skyed pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi 'od la gnas mi skye/ nga pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi chos bstan pa la gnas mi skyong ba yin/ 
62b6(phal chen): phyogs la gnas mi skyed pa yin/ phyogs mtshams la gnas mi skyed pa yin/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor la gnas mi skyed pa yin/ byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'ang 'dus pa la gnas mi

62b8(phal chen): la b.ras mi ltung ba yi / de banar pa shegs pa'i bzur ba ra ba la yang bskal pa brjo du byed pazang por byeng cing / sangs rgyas brjo mang po ma tho bas bskal ba grangs med par gnas kyang / sangs rgyas bldabs
63a1(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa mngon du bya ba dang / chos mnyan pas ngoms mi shes te/ sangs rgyas blta ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos mnyan pa la gnas mi spyong // byang chub sems dpa
63a2(phal chen): rgyan dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor dang / de bzhin gshegs pa khong du chud par byed kyang gnas mi skyed/ chags pa'i sems mi skye // 'jig rten gyi khams kun nas son mongs pa la zhugs kyang khong khro ba mi skyed
63a3(phal chen): mos pa med pa'i sems mi skye // de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar byang chub sems dpas ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos nyid ji lta ba bzhin du shin tu khong du chud de/ de la ni kun nas nyon mongs pa'ang med/ rnam par byang ba
63a4(phal chen): 'ang med/ mun pa'ang med/ snang ba 'ang med/ rnam par bya ba'ang mi da/ rnam pa tha dad pa'ang med/ rnam par rtog pa'ang med/ gzhan du 'gyur ba'ang med / bde ba yang med/ mi bde ba yang med lam yang med/

63b1(phal chen): gnas 'gro 'ang chags pa'i sems mi skyed de/ de dag la sems 'di ltar skyed // kye sangs rgyas kyi chos de lta gzung ba med/ sangs rgyas kyi byang chub de ltar sgrib pa med/ chos dang 'dul ba de ltar legs par bstan

63b4(phal chen): gyis brlabs kyang / byis pa so so'i skye bo 'di dag ni shes pa med pa/ mthong ba med pa/ tha dad pa med pa/ mos pa med pa/ mi mkhas pa/ ga nas la spyod pa/ bsam pa rmugs pa/ 'khor ba'i rgyud shin tu 'byung

63b6(phal chen): la drin du mi bzo ba/ dma' ba la gnas pa/ dngos po med pas 'jigs pa/ rigs pas spangs pa/ tshul bzhin ma yin pa la zhugs pa/ mnyam pa nyid las log par ltung ba/ g.yangs chen por rab tu ltung ba/ bdud kyi
63b7(phal chen): bsam pa la zhugs pa/ sangs rgyas kyi bsam pa las ring du gyur pa/ srid pa la mngon par chags pa sha sta go zhes/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems can gyi khams la 'jug cing / snying rje chen po de bas kyang
63b8(phal chen): cher bskyed nas/ snying rje chen po rgya cher byas te gnas med pa'i dge ba'i rtsabs/ dge ba'i rtsa ba yang dag par bsags nas/ 'di spam du sems bskyed // gal te sems can re re'i phyir yul re re dang / phyogs re re
64a1(phal chen): yang bskal pa brjod med par/ sems can re re 'dul ba'i phyir 'dug la/ sems can gcig la ji lta ba de bzhin du/ sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi don du 'dug kyang / bdag gis
64a2(phal chen): nga'i phyir mi dga' ba mi bskyed de/ yul de dang phyogs de nas kyang bdag gung du g.yo bar mi bya'o// gung tu 'gro bar mi bya'o// skra'i rtse mo tsam la chos kyi dbyings thams cad 'dus par bya ste/ skra'i rtse mo'i tshul de lta dus skra'i
64a3(phal chen): rtse mor chung pa re rer yang / sems can gyi khams yongasu smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba'i phyir bskal pa brjod maung ba'i yang brjod med par gnas par bya'o// skra'i rtse mo gcig la ji lta ba de bzhin du/ chos kyi dbyings
64a4(phal chen): mtha' dang dbus med pa thams cad la de ltar te/ se gol gtogs pa tsam du yang gnas kyi 'du shes mi bskyod// gnas par mi bya'o// gnas kyi sems mi bskyed// skra'i rtse mo tsam re re la yang lus gnas/

64b1(phal chen): ba'i mthu las byung bas/ 'jig rten thams cad sprul pa lta bur shes par bya'o// bdag gi spyod pa'i mthu las byung bas/ lus ni yid kyi rgyu las byung bar shes par bya'o// bdag gis sna tshogs dang / 'dres pa'i phyir
64b2(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad ni sems lta bur shes par bya'o// rnam par 'gyur ba med pas/ bdag gis chos thams cad ni yang dag pa'i mtha' mnyam par bstan par bya'o// bdag gis phyogs bcur sems bskyed pas
64b3(phal chen): rgyas par bkang ste/ chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa/ namakha'i mthas gtugs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la gnas par bya'o// bdag gis sems yang bar bsgyur ba dang / dran pa gnas med pa/ sangs rgyas
64b4(phal chen): kye chos khong du chud cing mkhas pa/ sems kyi skad cig gcig gis thob par bya'o zhes/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' de bdagang nga sangs rgyas la bdag med pa'i tshul gyis yang dag par lta cing
64b5(phal chen): sems can chags pa med pa'i mthar byin pa'i tshig gi lam gyis la smin par byed pa'i tshe/ dga' ba mtha' yas pa thob pa/ sangs rgyas dang rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos mos pa tshang
64b6(phal chen): med pa'ang yang dag par rab tu 'thob bo/ sems can thams cad yongasu bskyab pa'i don du bdag gis skyo ba'i sems mi bskyed // sems can gyi khams yongasu ma smin cing ma dul gyi bar du skye ba'i smod

64b8(phal chen): dang sems can le bar len pa dang / sems can rnam par gzhag pa dang / sems can gyi 'du shes dang ldan pa dang / sems can gyi glong dang / sems can gyi 'du byed dang / sems can gyi yul dang / sems ca

67b1(phal chen): rang nga ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi lam gyi rgyung las kyang mi g.yo'o// 'jig rten gnas pa'i drin du mi gzo bas yongasu gang ba dang / dgras yongasu grang ba dang / kun nas 'on mongs pas yongasu gang ba nga
67b2(phal chen): mi mthun pas yongasu gang ba dang / yid gzhag tu mi rung bsna yongasu gang ba dang / byis pas yongasu gang ba dang / ma dad pas yongasu gang ba dang / gzhan gyi drin la rgyug pas yongasu gang ba dang / shes rab ngan pas shin tu byung ba dang /

68a4(phal chen): gtam bya ba dang / lung bstan pa la spongs pa yin/ chos dang ldan pa'i gzungs thob pas ngon la spobs pa yin/ chos ji lta ba bzhi na gyi gzungs chos yang dag par skul pa thob pas chos la spobs pa yin/

72b5(phal chen): bo/ lha rdzas kyi rol mo'i sgra yang mngon par byung // lha rdzas kyis ngaba'ang rab tu byung // lha rdzas kyi sgra 'ang rab tu byung // gling bzhi pa 'di'i lha'i dbang po rab mtsho ma'i gnas na ji lta ba de bzhin
72b6(phal chen): phyogs bcu thams cad kyang rgyas par byas te/ thams cad na yang sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ chos 'di nyid bstan par spong // phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing brgya stong gi rdul shin tu phra ba sted
72b7(phal chen): 'das pa'i pha rol nas/ byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing brgya stong gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyeng 'ongs te/ phyogs bcu rgyas par byas nas 'di skad ces smraso// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de ltar khyod byang chub sems
72b8(phal chen): dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa'i chos nyid 'di ston pa leg so lagaso// kye rgyal ba'i sras bdag cag kun kyang yon tan dang ldan pa zhes bya ba dag ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan kun tu yon tan zhes bya ba dag gi
73a1(phal chen): phruras/ 'jig rten gyi khams yod tar gyi rgyal mtshan 'as bya ba mas byin te/ thams cadan yangasas rgyas kyi mthus 'khor 'di 'dra ba gan/ tshig 'di dag dang / mig 'di ga dang / bstan pa
73a2(phal chen): ga dang / ngor 'di cing brjod pas/ lhag chad med par chos bstar pa 'di ston to// kye rgyal ba'i bras/ de ltar bdag cag thams cad kyang / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis 'khor 'dir byin te/ ji ltar 'khor 'dir ba
73a3(phal chen): cag phyin pa de bzhin du/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rab mtshe ma'i gnas lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe ma'i khang pa nor bu sna tshogs shes bya ba kun tu yang
73a4(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing brgya stong rdul shin tu phra ba sbed par gyur to// / bam po nyi shu brgyad pa/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' yon tan dang ldan pas phyogs bcur bltas te/ 
73a5(phal chen): 'khor yong ba thams cad la rnam par bltas nas/ chos kyi dbyings la rnam par lta zhing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs yang / dag par gzung ba dang / khya chu ma 'o chub nga smon chu kyi sa rgya khyung
73a6(phal chen): ma / zug byu sa bya nga/ sa gro la tshul kyi rigs yang dag par gzung ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba ji ltar bskyed pa'i rgyur brjod pa dang / dus dang ji ltar 'byor pa'i yan lag dang / dbang po dang / bsam pa
73a7(phal chen): dang / mos pa dang / nyon mongs pa dang / ngag chags dang / sems dang / spyod pa dang / rnam pa g.yos pa'i rgyud thams cad yongasu brtag pa dang / sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rigs thams cad snang bar
73a8(phal chen): byed cing / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis/ de'i tshe tshig su bcid smras pa/ namakha'i lam gyi rlung gshegs shing / sgribs pa med par gzigs pa rdul rnams sbyangs gyur pa// kun tu mtha' yas spyod yul tsam
73b1(phal chen): stobs bcu mnga' ba de la phyag 'tsha'o// gang yang rgyal ba mi'i mchog/ chags pa mi mnga' yon tam tshad med mnga' ba ste// 'das dus mnyam pas macam gyur pa// rdul bstsal dngas spyod pa 'di yin// phyogs bcu'i 'jig
73b2(phal chen): na khams dag na// ngo mings pa gzigs pa brtar pa'i zhugs pa'i rnams// mtha' yas nyes pa kun bsal ba// gnas med de dag spyod pa 'di yino// chos dbyings bsam gyis mi khyab par// skyes bu'i seng ger
73b3(phal chen): rnams byon par mgyur pa// thugs rje che bskyed rnab spyod pa// phan mdzad de dag spyod pa 'di yi mo// dus gsum gzhal du med pa yi// rang byung gti mug rnam par bsal ba ji sbed pa// thams cad chos nyid mnyam bsdu
73b4(phal chen): stobs mnga' de dag spyod pa 'di yi no// gang rnams mtha' dbus med ba yi// 'jig rten khams kyi srid pa'i rgyud rnams rab gzigs shing // gzigs nas rtog pa mi mnga' ba// mi g.yo dag spyod pa 'di yin
73b5(phal chen): gang rnams chos kyi dbyings mkhyen cing // rnam dag don gyi dam pa gzig sa pa brtan pa rnams// gti mug tha ba nga rgyal sel ma dzang ba// legs mnga' de dag spyod pa 'di yi no// gang rnams sems
73b6(phal chen): kun mkhas shing // chos kyi dbyings la ngo bo nyid kyis zhugs gyur pa'i// bad gshegs gzhan dring mi 'jog pa// mamakha' mnyam pa da ltar spyod pa 'di yino// 'jig rten kun tu mtha' yas pa// mamakhas klas pa yang
73b7(phal chen): ngag thug su rung gyur te// zil gyis mi non chos mnga' ba// thub mchog de dag spyod pa 'di yino// ldog pa med pa de dag rnams// mi dma'i chos dang ldan pa thub par dka' ba dag/ smon las stobs kyi mthar phyin pa
73b8(phal chen): spyod rigs mnga' ba'i spyod yi pa lam par gyis/ mtha' dang bus mi med pa'i sor// rjes zhugs shing zang gzigs par gyur pa'i rnams// spyod yul zab mo mnga' ba yi// smra ba'i seng+ge'i spyod pa 'di mi
74a1(phal chen): / dbye ba'i tshig rgyus la// rje sa zhugs shing rgol ba 'dul bar mdzad pa yib// chos rnams rtogs pa mnga' ba'i rnams// thub chen de dag spyod pa 'di yin// 'jig rten bang bskyed mdzad cing // seM
74a2(phal chen): les med thugs dang ldan pa'i rnams// kha lo sgyur ba mnyam med pa'i// yon tan tshad med de dag spyod 'di yin// 'jigs pa med pa stobs mdzad cing // sems cad thams cad rab tu tshim par mdzad pa'i rnams/ 
74a3(phal chen): dang shing rnyog pa med pa yi// dpe med de dag spyod pa 'di yino// dge ba'i thugs dang ldan pa'i rnams// bsam pa rnam par dag cing spros pa med pa yi// dpal gyi gzi brjid spungs rgyas pa// dpa' mchog ldan pa de dag spyod
74a4(phal chen): 'di'o// don gyi pha rol phyin pa'i rnams// yon tan 'byung gnas rnam pa ra dag pa'i thugs mnga' ba// shin tu sems dpa'i blo ldan rnams// dri nas 'phags pa da ngag spyod 'di'o// bdag med 'ams pa mad
74a5(phal chen): ba'i rnams// rnga'i dbyangs rab mnga' ba zhing du gzhol ba dag/ chos kyi tshul la gnas pa'i rnams// tshig la khams med de dag su nga 'di'o// sbyin pas shin tu 'phags pa rnams// bsod nams mtshan rab
74a6(phal chen): brgyas kyang rab tu brgyan padag/ 'gro la phan par mdzad pa'i rnams// blo rab de dag spyod yul 'di yino// ye shes shin tu zab pa'i sar// rjesu zhugs shing blo gros shin tu brtan pa'i rnams// mi g.yo brdar zhing gnas pa
74a7(phal chen): / brtul zhugs brtan pa de dag spyod 'didzi'o// chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa yi// rjesu 'jug pa'i pha rol phyin par gyur pa dag/ rnam par 'phrul la brtson pa'i rnams// chos kyi mim de dag spyod 'di'o// mi ma ma
74a8(phal chen): mnyam pa'i sgom par rnams// mi gnyis yongasu bsgoms pa'i ting 'dzin ldan pa// bsas kau shin tu rtogs pa dag/ thams cad gzigs pa de dag spyod 'di'o// 'jig rten khams la rab 'jug pa// tha dang yangs pa
74b1(phal chen): tshe'i ma pa mas ca / srong yul rdzob par gyur ba'i rnams/ ye shes bong sa spyong 'anga'o// 'ong rungs pa'i sems lda pa/ 'ams rnams sasung po kun tu chags pa meng ba dag/ tshul khrims brgyal zhugs pa
74b2(phal chen): phyi ba// rnam dag sems ldan de dag spyod 'di'o// rnam pa'i dbyings kyis mthas gtugs pa'i// ye shes 'byam klas mngon par brjod pa la// shugs de bslangs pa'i blo ldan pa// ye shes stobs can de dag spyod 'di'o// 
74b3(phal chen): shes gsal ba'i phung po yis// dus gsum chos kyi dbyings rnams bkang ste sgrub byed kyang // sgying lug yi du mi 'gyur ba// sangs rgyas yul zhugs de dag spyod yulo// kun tu 'gro bar song gyur cing // stobs bcu mang
74b4(phal chen): ba'i chos rnams kun kyang shes pa'i rnams// lus kyi chos kyang chags ba ming// yon tan dpal can de dag spyod 'di'o// sems can mtha' dang dbus med pa// phyogs bcu 'jig rje mngag na rgyu bar gyur pa
74b5(phal chen): rnams// sems can kun gyi bdag ni skyabs yin pa// 'jigs med de ngag spyod pa 'di yi no// rtag par brtson 'grus gnas 'ama' zhing // nam yang sangs rgyas chos la zhum pa med pa'i rnams/ 
74b6(phal chen): 'jig rten sbyang phyir te// klu chen de dag spyod pa 'di yin// dbang po dag gi rgyus shes pa// mos pa'i tshul gyi pha rol phyin par gyur pa'i rnams// sna tshogs khams kyang rtogs gyur pa// mnyam med rtogs gyur de dag spyod
74b7(phal chen): 'di'o// phyogs rnams bcur bor chad med pa'i// mtha' dang dbus med rin chen mang pos 'gengs byed kyang // nam yang skyo ba'i yid med pa// dang par byed pa de dag spyod 'di'o// 'od zer dra ba mtha' yas pa// kun tu
74b8(phal chen): 'gyed cing 'jig rten snang bar byed pa'i rnams/ snang ba'i chos rnams rtogs gyur pa// blo gros bsgoms pa de dag spyod 'di'o// gang zhig phyogs bcu'i zhang gi rnams// khrag khrig bsam gyis mi khyab zang
75a1(phal chen): slo ba // 'jigs par 'gyur bar mi byed // 'jig chen pa pasrung ba chag tu 'arjon/ tshi su lamabs pa rnams brjong rnam par rgyu ba'i 'ayod byi rlung
75a2(phal chen): brjos meng ba bas papa/ mi sprul sems lngang ngag sbyong 'o// spyi chungs rgya mkhas pa pag// yang ya sa bar byabya ba'i pha ra phyin pa'i rangs// mazangs la sugs pa ga pas bye rje gros dngas
75a3(phal chen): 'di'o// yon tam khrag khrig mang meng ba// byang chub rab la gsol zhing spya ba spyod pa dag/ yon tan thams cad mthang byin pa// legs pa mi zang de ga spyod di 'o// 'jig rten las pa smra ba'i rnams// smu

75a8(phal chen): thams cad rgya yis rab tu 'debs byed pa// mtshan nyid med pa'i tshul ldan rnams// dpal gyi tshul can de dag spyod 'di'o// bde bar gshegs pa'i zhing gcig tu// bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dus rnams chung byed
75b1(phal chen): cing/ bskal ba grangs med 'dzud byed pa// skyo meng brtson pa de dag spyod 'di'o// tha dang mtshan can mi'i dbang // skra'i rtse mo gcig la sangs rgyas brjod yas pa// gang gis de dag mthong gyur rnams// spyod pa bzang ldan
75b2(phal chen): de dag spyod 'di'o// gang gis sna'i cha tsam la// brjod du med pa'i 'dren pa rnams ni mthong gyur cing // de bzhin chos dbyings thams cad de// rgyal sras de dag spyod pa 'di yin// bskal pa brjod med po'i rnams/

76a1(phal chen): skyong 'anga'o// 'jis can 'ams ni bcig nas kyang // deg 'dus gam mang 'tsho bar mi byed par// 'grob ku tu'ang blang ba'i rnams mtha' las chus ca de dag sbyong min/ ma

76b2(phal chen): char chen rab tu 'bengs shing zhing rnams yangs par rgyu// don rnams thams cad rtogs gyur pa// chos sprin de dag spyod yul 'di yin// ngad pa phyir ldog mi 'gyur zhing // rtsa ba shin tu tshugs shing dang pa rnam dag pa/

77a1(phal chen): pa'i tshung thobar// mas shig dang 'gyur// ma pa sa 'ang ga myong 'das// kung nga rab la bapas lda cang / chos mas ngas kun tu sa mas rim songs/
