78a1(phal chen): brgya sras ngas spong sa so// su stan la brgya byed pa/ ngas kyi rgol pa'i mam la lags par skyob pa/ mtha las tha'i rtsom pa// sa sa rgya tu tungasu rgyas pa sa
78a2(phal chen): mtha' thus me pa'i ming rnams// thas cad kA byung ba gcig gis bsal babyud // thas cang spang bar byeng pa'i mas// nunang se ba'i spyod 'di 'o// yang du rgyal bas nga 'os pa// nga ni sas khrag khring 'in tu 'a su byang sa
78a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas sdu dang sangs rgyas zhing // sangs rgyas rgyan ca khrag khrig snang bar byed/ spyod pa dag ni mtha' yas pa// su gnas brtan pa de dag shes par ji ltar rung // spyod pa thams cad shin tu stor// 'gro bar spyod pa thams cad mthar thug
78a4(phal chen): byed chos kyi dbyings dang ma sam pa yi// bdag gi lus ni brjod med par gyur pa yis// de dag legs pa brjod byas kyang // bskal pa khrag khrig ngag gis mi thong // yon tan kun tu mtha' yas shing // yon tan mchog rnam

103a7(phal chen): pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba mtha' yas pa brtan par mdzad pa/ sangs rgyas kyi cho 'phrul gzhal du med pa las byung ba/ tshig gi lam thams cad las yang dag par 'das pa/ byang chub sems dpa' rigs dang
103a8(phal chen): ldan pa thams cad kyis mngon par mos par bya ba/ sems can 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin du tshim par bya ba'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi sku yangs pa rje su khyab par gyur pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba brjod pa thams cad rnam par dag pas/ 
103b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi yon tan tshad med par yang dag par ston pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul rgyun mi 'chang bar 'byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi ting 'dzin las byung ba/ 'gro ba thams rang ma lus pa'i lus kyi rje su brangal ba/ sku'i byi
103b2(phal chen): gyi rlabs la sa mtshams med pa/ yid tshad med pa yongasu mgu bar mdzad pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rigs rgyun mi gcod pa/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa mtha' dang dbus med pa 'byung ba brnyes pa/ 'das pa dang / ma bya
103b3(phal chen): pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigasu byung ba/ khams dang / mos pa bgrang du med pa thams cad sbyong bar mdzad pa/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad ye shes mngon par bsgrub pa la 'jug par mdzad pa/ bang
103b4(phal chen): chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi dbang po rab tu dga' bar mdzad pa/ chos kyi sprin gyis namakha'i khams thams cad yog par mdzad pa/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad ma lus par de bzhin gshegs pas 'dul
103b5(phal chen): ba'i byin gyis rlabs kyis rlob pa/ sems can thams cad kyi rtog pa kha sam pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongasu rgyas par mdzad pa/ mi gnas pa 'i ye shes kyi rgyud kyis 'gro ba thams cad las 'phags pa/ ye
103b6(phal chen): shes kyi rnam pa thams cad brnyes pa/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs snang ba gzigs pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba ji ltar bskyed pa bzhin du yang dag par gzigs pa/ sems bskyed pa rgya chen po skye bar mdzad pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kun
103b7(phal chen): tu bzang po thug pa med pa'i ye shes yang dag par rgyu bas byung ba/ 'gro ba dang zhing thams cad khyab pa/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad mi ldog par gshegs pa/ sangs rgyas kyi sku'i rlung brjod med pa'i yang brjod med pa nga
103b8(phal chen): das par ston pa/ bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du 'dul pa mi mnga' bar byin gyis rlong pa/ 'gro bzed kyi tshig gi rnam pas yon tan mi zang ba/ sangs rgyas rjes dran pas/ chos kyi dbyings thams dang rgyas par mdzad pa/ 'jig
104a1(phal chen): rten gyi khams mtha' dang dbus med par khyab par mdzad pa/ byang chub kyi sems kyis/ ji ltar dam bcas pa'i sems can rim gror mdzad pa/ ji ltar brnyes pa'i chos kyi sbyin pa mdzad ga/ san
104a2(phal chen): ji ltar 'dul ba bzhin du 'dul bar mdzad pa/ mos pa dang bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par dag par mdzad pa/ gzugs kyi sku bsam gyis mi khyab par byin gyis rlob pa/ 'gro ba thams cad la gnas pa mi mnga' zhing mtha
104a3(phal chen): bzhid kyi rje su bzhung ba/ spong ba tha dad pa las byung ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu bsgribs pa med pa/ mngon par sangs rgyas pa/ thugs la chags pa mi mnga' bas rtag tu mkham par bzhag cing ma 'dres pa/ sa
104a4(phal chen): thams cad la rnam par spyod pa/ don dang tshig dang yi ge tha dad pa yang dag pa ra ston pa/ ye shes rgya mtsho mtha' dang dbus med pa la zhugs pa/ yon tan gyi mchog ye shes kyi snying pos byung ba/ chos kyi dbyings
104a5(phal chen): thams cad sangs rgyas kyi lim shar ba/ 'gro ba thams cad sngon gyi spon lam zad pa mi mnga' bar chos kyi dbyings kyi rang bzhin la gan sa pa/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spong ba ma nyams pa b.ras pa/ 
104a6(phal chen): bdag gi dang yongasu gzung ba med pas gnas pa mi mnga' ba/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos tha~Mng 'byung zhing / 'jig rten gyi chos thams cad kyis ma gos pa 'gro ba thaMd kyi mi shes pa'i rgyal mtshan yang dag par
104a7(phal chen): bcang ba/ 'jig rten thaMd kyi mi shes pa chen po yongasu bsal ba'i gnasu gyur pa/ 'gro ba thams cad snang bar mngon par 'don pa/ 'jig rten thang ye shes khyab par du 'phags pa la rab tu gzhog pa/ 'gro ba zad
104a8(phal chen): sebar 'tsho ba'i bsong dpas yong su mi ba ba/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyigs pa zug du chung bas dang bang bya ba 'os pa/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgya su gzhol ba'i byams pa chen po las rgyas
104b1(phal chen): thugs rje chen po yang dag par ston pas spyod pa/ sangs rgyas kyi sku brjod du med pa'i chos dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos sna tshogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i gsung dang dbyangs kyi char 'bebs pa/ sems can gyi bsam pa ji lta
104b2(phal chen): ba bzhin du yang dag par tshim par mdzad pa/ sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha' dang / da ltar byung ba'i mtha' rings pa'i byin rlangs shin tu dag cing bsam gyis mi khyab pas sems can dag par mdzad pa/ byang chu
104b3(phal chen): sems dpa' thams cad lung bstan pa rgyun mi 'chang nga/ sangs rgyas kyi rigasu dbang bskur ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rgyu du byung ba/ 'jig rten thams cad 'khor lo mi ldog par 'khor ba/ 'jig rten thams cad
104b4(phal chen): kyi mngor bar zher pa thams cad las 'phags pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi mtha' klas pa la mi gnas pa/ 'gro ba thams cad mnyam pa ci du thugasu chung ba/ 'jig rten las
104b5(phal chen): 'das pa'i bsod nams kyis rnam par dag pa/ 'khor ba la mi bzhugs par 'jig rten thams cad snang bar gyur pa/ btsal ba mi dmigs pas/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi rang bzhin ye
104b6(phal chen): shes kyi zla ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa tshad med pa'i rjesu bzhud pa/ sgyu ma lta bu'i ye shes kyis byin gyis rlob pa/ mig yor lta bu'i ye shes kyis rnam par ston pa/ rmi lam lta bur rjesu dran pa/ sprul pa dang ma'am
104b7(phal chen): bar thung ba/ sems kyi rang ba'ir lta bur 'jig rten sna tshogs thams cad byin gyis rlob pa/ las kyi rnam par smin pa'i tshul dang / bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du/ sems can gyi skye mched rnam par phye ba yang
104b8(phal chen): dab par ston pa/ sems can gyi dbang po dang 'thur par sangs rgyas kyi sku thung ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i dmigs pa la sems can grangs med pa'i mas kyang dag par gnas pa/ 'jig rten thams cad rten cing
105a1(phal chen): 'brel bar 'thung ba rnam par bstad pa'i rang bzhin du/ chos kyi mtshan nyid kyis yang dag par spyod pa/ ye shes kyi rgyud mtshan ying meng pa'i rang bzhin dang / mtshan cing gcig tu gyur pa/ 
105a2(phal chen): 'jig rten thams cad kyi rang bzhin gyi mtshan nyid snang ba mngon par bsgrub pa'i spyod pa yang dag par ston cing / 'gro ba thams cad gdon par brtson pa/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod yul bla na med pa yang dag par stor pa/ 'dzi/ 
105a3(phal chen): rten dang zhing thams cad yongs skyob pas/ sangs rgyas kyi mtshan ma gzung bar 'jig rten du mngon par byung ba/ 'jig rten gyi nyon mongs pa'i mtshan ma thams cad rnam par bstsal pa/ 'jig rten thams cad kyi rjesu dran pa
105a4(phal chen): dang / dmigs par 'byor par gyur pa/ 'khrug pa med pa/ khong du chud par 'gyur ba'i rgyu theg pa chen pos zhal yongs rgyas pa/ chos thams cad kyi don grub pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa bas rnam pa
105a5(phal chen): bye ba nyams pa med pa'i 'drin las rnam par smin pas rnam par dag pa ye shes kyi 'thung gnas dus gsum mnyam pa ci du thug du chung pa/ 'jig rten thams cad kyi yongasu rtog pa/ yongasu mi rtog pas
105a6(phal chen): zung ba/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'od zer gyi dra bas bsal bar gyur pa/ phyogs bcu 'byam klas pa thams cadadu sangs rgyas kyi 'od gyis snang bar mdzad pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rje su bzhud pa balnga
105a7(phal chen): bas mi ngoms shing btang mi phra ba/ yon tan chen po dang / ye shes dang / mngon par shes pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa 'byung ba/ dbang po mngon par mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul can/ ye shes kyi
105a8(phal chen): dkyil 'khor gyis sangs rgyas kyi mdzad brgyas par mdzad pa/ sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las shin tu sgrub pa nu cing 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i tshul ston pa byang chub
105b1(phal chen): sems dpa'i gzungs mtha' yas pa'i char 'debs pa/ bsam pa yangs pa'i bsgom pa yongasu 'dzin par mdzad pa/ sangs rgyas kyi dpal thams cad kyis rab tu 'bar ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku kha dog mtha' yas
105b2(phal chen): pa sna tshog su 'jig rten thams cad la mngon par ston pa/ sgrib pa'i chos thams cad ma lhung ba/ chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin gyis dor gyis dag pa/ yon tan gyi chos thams cad la mnga' bas/ mdzes pa'i dkyil
105b3(phal chen): 'khor can/ yon tan gyi 'od zer mnga' ba'i nyi mar gyur pa/ bsod nams kyi zhing du shar ba/ gzi brjid thams cad kyi dra bas mngon par skyes pa/ 'jig rten thams cad sangs rgyas kyis sprul pa yang dag par
105b4(phal chen): 'dzin pa/ 'jig rten thams cad sprul par thug su chung ba'i ye shes snang ba dang ldan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i go 'phang chags pa med pa mnga' ba phyi ma'i mtha'i yon tar 'jig rten thams cad kyi rnam par shes pa/ 
105b5(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad dang 'thun bar stor pa'i ye shes kyi phyag mngar/ pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa ye shes kyi sman pa/ sems can thang bde bar mdzad pa/ 'jig rten chang med pa thams cad shin
105b6(phal chen): tu rnam par dag pas rjesu 'brang ba/ 'gro ba dang zhing 'byam klas pa thams cad phyir mi ldog pa/ ye shes kyi spyan phungs rab rib med cing rnam par dag pa/ sangs rgyas kyi lo legs pa yang dag par ston pa 'bru
105b7(phal chen): ba'i sems can gyi khams la su rung bar mdzad pa/ 'dul ba sna tshogs du ma la 'jug pa/ dus bzhin du 'dul ba'i rgyun mi 'chad pa/ 'gro ba thams cad la mnyam pa'i thugs kyis yang dag par spyod pa las/ skyon med
105b8(phal chen): pa'i rnam par spor ba dang / mya ngang las las pa yang dag par ston pa bsam pa dang / las dang rdzu 'thur ba'i 'bras bu ji lta ba bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi sku ras par spong ba/ sangs rgyas kyi sku ji lta ba bzhin du sems ca
106a1(phal chen): kyis chos shes pa 'byung bar mdzad pa/ sangs rgyas kyis sprul pa byin gyis rlob pa/ 'jig rten gyi chos thams cad la rnam par gzigs pa'i ye shes mnga' ba/ dga' ba chen pong
106a2(phal chen): lhag pa'i bsam pas dbang po dga' bar mdzad pa/ sangs rgyas mthong ba'i ngang pa'i shugs mtha' yas pas byung ba/ sems can tha~Md kyi rang gi dge ba'i rtsa ba phyir mi ldog par mdzad pa/ sems cad kyi las ji lta ba
106a3(phal chen): bzhin du rje su 'brang ba/ 'gro ba gnyis kyis log pa thams cad sad par mdzad pa/ sangs rgyas skye bas dge ba yang dag par 'phel ba mdzad pa/ sems can la sangs rgyas kyi bag dbab pa/ chen po stobs pa mdzad
106a4(phal chen): pa/ 'jig rten gyi lta ba thams cad la mi gnas pa/ ye shes kyi don la rab tu gzhog pa/ rab tu gzhag pa'i ye shes kyi tshul gyi spyod yul thug su chung ba/ sangs rgyas kyis gzigs pa'i zil gyis ma
106a5(phal chen): non pa'i rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ chos kyi rgyud drugasu chung ba'i ri bo rnam par dag pa/ sangs rgyas 'byam klas pa dang / byang chub sem sadapa' gzhan dang gzhan du ston/ kha na ma tho ba med pa'i sa la sen
106a6(phal chen): rab tu 'gro dang / sangs rgyas kyi yon tan grangs med pas rnam par bris pa/ las kyis sna tshogasu gyur pa'i 'jig rten du/ de bzhin gshegs pa sna tshogs yang dag par ston pa/ sangs rgyas kyi 'thung gnas rnamapa
106a7(phal chen): sbyong ba/ ye shes thams cad yongasu 'thob par mdzad pa/ 'jig rten thams cad kyi smon lam rjesu srung ba/ mi shigs pa/ 'gro ba thams cad la dge ba'i bshes gnyen ston pa/ snang ba dri ma med cing mchog tu dag par
106a8(phal chen): mdzang ba/ 'gro ba ma lus pa thams cad kyis ji tsam du mngon sum du mthong ba de tsam du brjod med pa/ sems can thams cad kyi 'gro ba'i rjesu song ba'i byin gyi rlabs mngara' ba/ grogs sngon du 'gro ba'i dge ba'i
106b1(phal chen): rtsangs/ sems can rnam par dag par mdzad pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi smon lam gyi rjesu song ba/ nyams pa med pa/ sems can thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba yongasu bzung bas dag par mdzad pa las bstsags pa'i tshul
106b2(phal chen): gyis yongasu byung ba/ bdud kyi dkrugs ma thams cad rnam par 'jom par byung ba/ chags pa med pa'i mtha'i stobs kyis byung ba/ 'gro ba thams cad kyis blta na 'od shin tu dang bar snang ba ye shes kyi dbyings chags pa
106b3(phal chen): med pa'i snying po'i nyi ma sems can gang yang rung ba la chos kyi sbyin pa mdzad pa/ 'od zer gyi dkyil 'khor gyi mdzod mtha' dang dbus med pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs kyi ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor mnga' ba/ 
106b4(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad la snang bar gyur pa/ bsam pa dang yang dag par rtogs pa thams cad yongasu rdzogs pa/ phyir rgol ba shin tu bcom pa/ yon tan gyi gnas dam pa mchog tu gyur pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi
106b5(phal chen): du gyur pa/ yon tan tshad med par 'gyur ba 'gro ba thams cad yongs dag par mdzad pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba chung ngu tshad med par yong su 'dzin pa/ zang mi shes pa'i ye shes kyi sar 'dzud cing rab
106b6(phal chen): du gnog pa/ 'jig rten thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba sems la rag lus par yid ches pas/ tshad med pa'i bsod nams dang yon dag par mdzad pa/ ye shes kyi tshul gyis ngan song gsum gyi 'gro ba yongasu skyong
106b7(phal chen): pa'o zhes rnam pa de la bung / de bzhin gshegs pa la mos pa rnam pa de lta bur yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la yang dag par lta ga rnam pa de lta bung ye shes kyi mu stegs las 'bab pa rnam pa des
106b8(phal chen): bu'i yon 'an rgya mtsho'i gangs chen mtsho thams cad la 'jug pa/ rnam pa lta bu'i ye shes kyi namakha'i rjesu phyin par rjesu 'gro ba rnam pa de lta bur 'gro ba thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing du yang dag pa ji
107a1(phal chen): par shes pa rnam pa de lta bur de bzhin gshegs pa dran pa'i spos lta ba/ rnam pa de lta bur dge ba'i 'phrin las rnam par dag pa'i mtshan cing phun sum tshogs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa la
107a2(phal chen): rtog pa// rnam pa de lta bu'i yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi sku chen po/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad snang bar byed pa/ rnam pa de lta bu'i nga bzhin gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa thams
107a3(phal chen): cang yang dag par bstar par rjesu sems pa de dag gis/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku/ bcom ldan 'das kyi ba spu'i sgo ra re nas 'od zer bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa 'byung ba grangs med par rnam par dag pa/ 
107a4(phal chen): grangs med par shin tu snang ba/ grangs med par bltar yod pa/ grangs mang ba'i sems can gyi dga' ba skyed pa/ grangs med pa'i spro bskyed pa/ grangs med pa'i sangs rgyas la 'dun pa rnam pa 'phes
107a5(phal chen): bar byed pa/ grangs med pa'i lhag pa'i bsam pa rnam par sbyong ba/ grangs med pa'i dbang po sim par byed pa/ grangs med pa'i nge zhin gshegs pa'i spyod yul thob par byed pa mang po mthong bar
107a6(phal chen): gyur to// 'od kyi 'khor lo bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong bsam gyis mi khyab pa yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku las rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs kyis 'phrul zhing 'byung ba/ kha dog bsam gyis mi khyab pa// mdog
107a7(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ 'od bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbus med pa/ thams cad rgyas par byed pa/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs dang / sems can rnam par dag pas/ dri zhim por rab tu
107a8(phal chen): byung ba/ tshig su bcang ba bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong bsam gyis mi khyab pa yongasu 'dzin pa/ 'jig rten thams cad las rnam par 'das shing / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dge ba'i rtsa bas yongasu zung ba rgya bye/ 
107b1(phal chen): da khrag khrig brgya stong bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ yang dag par ston pa/ bskal nga bye ba khrag khrig bsam gyis mi khyab par yon tan mi zad pa/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul bzang mi shes pa las zung ba/ sangs rgyas
107b2(phal chen): skye ba brjod med pa yang dag par ston pa/ ye shes kyi sgo la rab tu gnog pa/ don yangs pa shin tu ston pa/ sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa brjod med pa'i tshul yang dag par ston pa/ sangs rgyas kyi yul mtha' dang dbas
107b3(phal chen): thong ba/ chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa/ na mkha'i khams kyi mthar thug pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad byin gyis rlabs kyis byung ba/ 'gro ba thams cad rnam par dag pa/ mnyam pa nyid kyi rjesu song ba/ 
107b4(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa chags pa med pa/ mtha' dang dbus med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi spyod ba las byung ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pas brten pa'i dpal yod pa/ rin po che'i 'od 'phro ba
107b5(phal chen): bye ba brgya stong bsam gyis mi khyab pa ltar byung ba mthong bar gyur to// bcom ldan 'das kyis kyang byin gyis rlabs kyis rgyar smon lam chen po las byung ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba mtha' yas pa
107b6(phal chen): dang / de bzhin gshegs pa mchis par bya ba'i spyod pas rnam par dag pa dang / sngon gyi bag yod pa las yang dag par byung ba'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i sems chags pa med pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba las byung ba dang / 
107b7(phal chen): de bzhir gshegs pa 'byam klas pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi the tsom gcod pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ba la sems can tshad med pa rab tu dgong ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba'i sgo dang / sangs rgyas kyi tshe
107b8(phal chen): 'phrul zil gyis nor pa med pa la/ rgya mtsho'i mthas gtugs pa'i sems can gzung bar bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' bka' bzhin byed pa thams cad sangs rgyas kyi zhing kun nas 'dus pa dang / sangs rgyas
108a1(phal chen): kyi byin gyis rlabs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos bsam gyis mi khyab pa yongasu brjod pa'i tshul gyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor du ji ltar sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'byam klas pa khrag
108a2(phal chen): khrig brgya stong brjod med pa grangs med pa dag na/ sems ma dad pa rnams dad par bya ba dang / sems dad pa'i rnams rnam par 'phel bar bya ba dang / sems rnam par 'phel ba'i rnams rnam par dag par bya ba dang / 
108a3(phal chen): sems rnam par dag pa'i rnams yongasu smin par bya ba dang / sems yongasu smin pa'i rnams 'dul bar bya ba dang / chos zab mo khong du chud par bya ba dang / ye shes snang ba mtha' dang dbus med par khong du chud
108a4(phal chen): par bya ba dang / sems tshad med pa'i rnams rgya che bar bya ba dang / thams ca dra mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa las phyir mi ldog par bya ba dang / chos nyid dang mi 'gal bar bya ba dang / yang dag pa'i mthas mi
108a5(phal chen): sdug par bya ba dang / de bzhin cing rab tu rtogs par bya ba dang / pha rol tu phyin pa'i rnams kyang rab tu rdzogs par bya ba dang / 'dzi garten las 'das pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par sbyang bar bya ba dang / 
108a6(phal chen): dmigs pa thams cad la brtson pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul ba yang kun tu bzang po'i tshul du mos par bya ba dang / bdud kyi yul las rnam par ldog par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi yul 'thob par bya ba dang / 
108a7(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos nyid shes par bya ba dang / ye shes bsam gyis mi khyab pa skye bar bya ba dang / theg pa chen po'i smon lam las phyir mi ldog par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas blta ba las mi 'bang bar bya ba
108a8(phal chen): dang / ye shes khong du chud par bya ba tshad med pa rtogs par bya ba dang / sa mtshams med pa'i bsod nams kyi stobs yang dag par yong su bsgrub par bya ba dang / shin tu dga' ba'i sems bskyed par bya ba dang / 
108b1(phal chen): the tshom med pa'i sa la 'jug par bya ba dang / kha na ma tho ba med cing yongasu dag pa 'thob par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la rten pa so sor thob par bya ba dang / chos mthong ba las phyir mi ldog par bya ba dang / byang chub sems
108b2(phal chen): dpa' thams cad kyi tshogs kyi rje su 'jug par bya ba dang / dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs grub par bya ba de lta de ltar/ bcom ldan 'das kyis thugs rje chen po kun tu khyab pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i
108b3(phal chen): ye shes kyi phung po chen pos byin gyi rlabs kyi rgyan rnam pa tha dad pa mang po yang dag par ston to// de ltar bcom ldan 'das kyis sems can thams cad 'dul ba'i dbang du sangs rgyas kyi bdag nyid che ba brjod pa'i phyir/ chags
108b4(phal chen): ba med pa'i ye shes kyi snying po rab tu snang bas sangs rgyas kyi dpal mtha'as sang rab tu 'bar ba/ sangs rgyas kyi cho 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab pas rnam par snang ba thams cad brdung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i

114a1(phal chen): kyi dus gsum gyi yon tan tshang med pa dang ldan pa sha stag/ de bzhin gshegs pa mngor sum du bya ba dang / sangs rgyas 'byam klas pa thams cad blta ba'i phyir kun nas 'dus par
114a2(phal chen): gyur to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan gyis sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smraso// yang dag sangs rgyas skye ba med// rgyal
114a3(phal chen): ba mya ngan mi 'da' ste// rgyu 'thun pa'i smon 'am gyis// des ni rnam par 'phrul pa snang // 'di dag chos ni bsam mi khyab// 'di dag sems kyi spyod yul min// gang gis ye shes pha rol phyin// des ni sangs
114a4(phal chen): rgyas spyod yul mthong // lus 'di yang dag sangs rgyas min// sgra 'ang de bzhin gshegs pa min// lus dang sgra las gzhan na yang // sangs rgyas rnam par 'phrul mi mthong // sngon gyi las rnams
114a5(phal chen): ma gtogs par// rang thung rnams kyi spyod yul gyi// mchog gi chu la rnams shes pa ni// brog zhan rnams kyis mi nuso// yang nga ga sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul 'di// gang dag nas kyang ma 'ongs te/ 
114a6(phal chen): du'ang 'gro bar mi 'gyur ro// 'di dag rang byung skra yin no// tshad med shin tu 'dren pa rnams// chos 'di rab tu bshad mdzad kyang // chos la gnas pa gang yang med// zhing rnams bye ba kun na snang // mkhyen pas
114a7(phal chen): mthar dang dpung med de// chos kun thugasu chud cing rtogs// chos kyi dbyings la rab zhugs nas// rnam par 'phrul ba ston pa mdzad// chos rnams kun la chags pa med// 'gro la de ni bsgribs mi mngar/ 
114a8(phal chen): tshad med pa yi yon tan gyis// zhing rnams kun na rab tu snang // gang zhig ye shes 'di dag dang // ye shes thams cad rtogs 'dod pas// bsam pa rnam par sbyang byas to// byang chub spyod pa spyang par bya/ 
114b1(phal chen): drang song chen po'i byin gyis rlabs// 'di 'dra gang gis mthong gyur cing // de ni the tsom mi byed na// dge ba shes mchog la brjed pa yin// de nas byang chub sems dpa' dam pa'i rgyal mtshan gyis// sangs rgyas kyi
114b2(phal chen): byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshigasu bcang pa 'di dag smraso// shin tu zab ste brjodadu med// brjod du yod kyang 'da' bar dka'// tshig lam las shin tu 'das// namakha' la
114b3(phal chen): ni rgyal ba snang // de bzhi gshegs pa'i byin rlabs kyis// mi'i seng ge mthong bar 'gyur// yang dag sangs rgyas rtog med kyang // rgyal ba rnam par rtog par snang // 'jig rten mgon pos chos nyid
114b4(phal chen): dngos// zengab mo 'di dag yang dag bstan// gang zag mtshungs pa med pa yi// des ni sku 'dir rab tu 'byung // thams cad gzigs kyi spyod yul gyi// ye shes chen po 'di 'dra ste// 'di la gang zhig
114b5(phal chen): rtogs 'dod pa// des na rgyal ba mngon du byos// yid kyi dbang po rnam dag bla// de bzhin gshegs pa bsnyen bkur zhing // 'di'i tshul les 'da' byed tshe// nam yang skyo bar mi bya'o// 
114b6(phal chen): mi zad pa'i bsod nams dang // byang chub sems kyis brtan pa'i rnams// the tsom rnam par bzlog byas te// de dag la ni skyo med ltos// rgyal sras gang gis chos dbyings kyi// shin tu bstan
114b7(phal chen): mthar phyin pa// des ni kun gzigs rnam 'phrul pa// 'di dag shin tu 'da' bar bya// dad pa chos 'di'i rtsa ba zhes// chos kyi phung pos bshad mdzad kyis// dad pa shin tu cher skyed la/ 
114b8(phal chen): byang chung spyod ba spyad par gyis// sangs rgyas kyi snang bar byed cing // de bzhin gshegs 'dril gabab// yang dag sangs rgyas dpal ldan las// de dag rgyang mar mi gnaso// bdag nyid che ba 'di lta bu// gang zhig thos mthong
115a1(phal chen): malas pa rnams// spyod yul thob par cir 'gyur ba'i// smon lam su thig song sa byed// de nas byang chub sems dpa' dpa' ba'i rgyal mtshan gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur
115a2(phal chen): par bltas nas/ de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smraso// ji ltar phyi ma'i 'od sdang bas// mig gris gzugs rnams mthong gyur pa// de bzhin sangs rgyas byin rlabs kyis// dag pa'i sems ldan rgyal ba mthong // ji ltar brtson 'grus
115a3(phal chen): spobs ldan pa// rgya mtsho la ni 'jug par byed // de bzhin ye shes spobs ldan pas// bsam du med pa'i sangs rgyas mthong // ji ltar sa bon rnam pa dag/ zhing bzang la ni skyer 'gyur ba// de bzhin sems bsam rnam dgal// sangs
115a4(phal chen): rgyas chos ni skye bar 'gyur// ji ltar nor gyi phung po yis// dbul ba thaMd spong byed pa// de bzhin sangs rgyas chos rnams kyis// byang chub sem sa dpa' rnam dag 'gyur// ji ltar dug tu gyur pa la// nad med dug
115a5(phal chen): sAr rgyal bar byed// de bzhir cor mongs rnam pa la// rnam dag tshul ni spyod yulo// sangs rgyas kyis ni gang bsngags pa'i// dge ba'i bshes la brten byas na// de yi mthus ni sangs rgyas kyi// chos ca
115a6(phal chen): 'di dag thos par 'gyur// bskal pa bye ba grangs med par// sbyin pa mchog rnams sbyin byas kyang // 'di'i tshul la rab spyod pa'i// grangs dang char yang mi 'gro'o// sangs rgyas yon tan mtha' yas te// mtshan gyis shin
115a7(phal chen): rnam par bris// brjod pas yang dag sangs rgyas rnams// rgyal ba shes par mi nuso// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rkang gnyis mchog/ gnas nas g.yo ba mi mnga' bar// sku ni kun tu rnam rgyu ming // chos kyi dbyings ni ston pa mdzad/ 
115a8(phal chen): ji ltar rnam pa'i khams 'di ni// nam yang rang bzhin mi 'gyur te// de bzhin sangs rgyas chos nyid kyang // ngo bo nyid las 'gyur ba med// de nas byang chub sems dpa' skar ma'i rgyal mtshan gyis// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs
115b1(phal chen): kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa 'di dag spraso// mi'i 'jig rten 'di kun dang // lha'i gnas rnams thang dang // 'gro ba ma lus kun na yang // mi'i gtso bo shin tu snang // ji ltar sems dngos gcig
115b2(phal chen): pu las// rnam pa tha dad sems brjod pa// de bzhin sangs rgyas sku gcig las// sangs rgyas thams cad brjod pa yin// byang chub gnyi su med par brjod// byang chub de yang mtshan cing med// mtshan gyis mngon par rnam bris pa'i/ 
115b3(phal chen): sku rnams gnyi su snang bar gyur// mkha' dang chos kyi dbyings la zhugs// sgyu ma'i sa yang rab tu bstan// de phyir sangs rgyas de dag gi/ spyod yul blta bzang ba med// yang dag sangs rgyas chos kyi sku// mgon po thams cad
115b4(phal chen): dus gsum du// ji ltar 'dul ba'i 'gro ba la// gzugs kyi skur yang rab tu snang // 'di 'dra'i lus su bdag gyur ces// sangs rgyas rtog/ par mi mdzad// ston la rnam rtog mi mnga' yang // byin gyi rlabs
115b5(phal chen): ston par mdzad// dbyer med pa'i dbyings la yang // chos kyi dbyeng sa ni yang dag gnas// 'jig rten khams ni tshang med par// thu babs rnam par rtog pa bstan// sku ni sprur pa ma yin te/ sprul min
115b6(phal chen): 'ang sku ma yin// sprul pa med pa'i chos 'di yis// sprul pa rnams ni rab tu bstan// yang dag sangs rgyas tshad med pa// chos kyi dbyings la shin tu chen// mtha' dang dpung med rab tu zab// tshig gi 'am gyis bzlal
115b7(phal chen): dka'// kun tu 'gro ba'i chos rnams la// de bzhin gshegs pa don nges mkhyen// zhing rnams kun la chags mi mnga'// chos kyi dbyings la rnam par spyod// de nas byang chub sems dpa' ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis/ 
115b8(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlangs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smraso// kun mkhyen ye shes ma chags pa// de la zhugs par gang gyur pa// de'i sems ni tshang mi zin// byang chub kyi spyad pa
116a1(phal chen): spyod// de bzhin gshegs pa mang po rnams// yul dang yul du de snang // chos rnams phyogs gcig gang la yang // yang dag sangs rgyas gnas pa med// 'jig rten sgro ma de dag gis// byin
116a2(phal chen): gyi rlangs ni gang bstan pa// bskal pa bsam gyis mi khyab par// 'di'i mtha' ni rung bar dka'// dus gsum rnams ni ji sbed ba'i// sems can rnams kyi mthar thug pa// bgrang ba'i mthar ni phyin par nus// 
116a3(phal chen): 'dren pa la ni mthar thug med// de dag sku ni gcig tu snang // sku rinyas de dag bsam mi khyab// 'jig rten khabasu sdang gyur kyang // sku la gnyisu gyur pa med// ji ltar zla ba shar gyur pa// tshad med pa'i gzugs
116a4(phal chen): brgyan rnams// chu'i snong snang gyur kyang // zla ba gnyi su gyur pa med// bzhin chags med ma khyer ldan rnams// chags med rnam par 'chang/ ga// ming rnams kun na rab tu snang/ sangs rgyas la ni gnyis kya
116a5(phal chen): meng/ 'di la gcig kyang yong ma yin// sku ni gnyis sam gsum du med// ji ltar sems can bsam pa bzhin// tshad med par ni rab tu snang // sku ni 'das pa ma yin te// ma 'ongs pa'ang sgyu ma yin/ 
116a6(phal chen): skyes dang byang chub mya ngan 'das/ skad gcig gis ni rab tu snang // ji ltar sgyu mar gyur pa'i gzugs// skyes pa ma yin 'ongs pa min// de lta de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku// skye ba med par shin tu bstan// de nas byang chub
116a7(phal chen): sems dpa' rin po che'i rgyal mtshan gyis// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa 'di dag spraso// yang dag sangs rgyas tshad med par// chadu sku yang rnam par bstan
116a8(phal chen): ji ltar 'dul ba'i semams sa// de bzhin 'dren pa rab tu mthong // sku laphyogs ni med par brjod// sangs rgyas yul ni ma lus khyab// par sna mas pa 'ji lta ba// de bzhin sangs rgyas bsam mi khyab// de ba'i sems
116b1(phal chen): kyang 'pho ba meng // sems la skye ba yod pa'ang min// sangs rgyas rnams kyi spyod yul ni// skye ba med la rab tu gnas// ji ltar rang rib ldan pa'i mig/ nang na med cing phyi na'ang med// de bzhin 'jig rten sangs rgyas dag/ na
116b2(phal chen): mi bzhugs phyi na'ang min// 'jig rten kun don gyi phyir// rkang gnyis kyi ni mchog byung ste// 'jig rten du ni ma byung yang // 'jig rten dag tu skye bos mthong // sangs rgyas rnams la zhing mi gnas// rgyal ba dag la yin
116b3(phal chen): mtshan med// skad cig ma yin zla ba min// rgyal ba la ni lo mi gnas// 'jig rten dag na ji skad brjod// nyi ma che ge mo zhig tu// rang byung byang chub rgyal bas thob// sangs rgyas kyi ma'i rjes mi 'brang // de la bskal
116b4(phal chen): yong ma yin// dus kyang ma lus med pa ste// dus gsum yang dag rdzo gas sangs rgyas// mgon po rnams ni mnga' bar 'gyur// ji ltar ma'i dkyil 'khor ni// nabs kyang mtshan dang mi gnas te// nyin mtshan
116b5(phal chen): zhes kyang rab tu brjod// de bzhin sangs rgyas chos nyi // bskal pa gcig dang dus gsum du// 'dren pa bzhugs pa ma yin te// dus gsum zhes kyang rab tu brjod// sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos cid
116b6(phal chen): bltos// de nas byang chub sems dpa' rdul dang bral ba'i rgyal mtshan gyis sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs bcad pa 'di dag smra so// yang dag sangs rgyas sku gcig ste/ 
116b7(phal chen): 'dren pa thams cad dor gcig kyang // chang med gzhan dang gzhan dag tu// phyogs bcu kun na rab tu snang // gang gis ma lus thams cad kyi// chos kyi dbyings rnams kun khyab pa// sen gtso bor thub pa yis// spyod
116b8(phal chen): yub rnams ni ci 'dra ltos// sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos cid ni/ kanang gi skus kyang snang ba yin// de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis rlabs// phyi rol grus kyang mi snang // dus mang kun du las rnams kyis// ji sngar sa
117a1(phal chen): rnams bsugs pa badzin// da ba'ir sor bye ba'i skus// rig su byung bar rab tu bstad// rgyal ba'i chos cings gtogs par// sangs rgyas sku ni 'di 'dra ba// grangasu bgrang bar mi nus te/ @
117a2(phal chen): bas lha yang shes mi nus// ji ltar bdag cag sebs kyi las// bsam gyis mi khyab mi 'byung ba// de bzhin sangs rgyas bsam mi khyab// sems kyi 'phrin las mi mnga'o// ji ltar cing rnams bsam yas pa/ 
117a3(phal chen): sa la rnam par dag pas mdzes// de bzhin sangs rgyas bsam mi khyab// 'gro ba dag na mdzes par snang // ji ltar las rnams 'jug pa ni// rkyen gyis rab tu 'byung bar 'gyurapa// de bzhin rgyu rnams 'thun pa las// 
117a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas shin tu mthong bar 'gyur// yid bzhin nor bu'i rgyal po ni// ji ltar yid bsam rdzogs byed pa// de bzhin sangs rgyas chos nyid kyang // rtag tu smon lam rdzogs par sgrub// mtha' dang dpung med
117a5(phal chen): 'jig rjer 'dir// 'jig rten mgon po 'dren par gyur// de'i smon lam de dag gis// phyogs bcu 'di dag rgyal bas gang / de nas byang chub sems dpa' dri ma med ba'i rgyal mtshan gyis//

117a7(phal chen): rnam sbyangs nas// sangs rgyas chos rnams rab tu brjod// de ste sems can mnyam sangs rgyas// sems can la las bsam byas na// rgyal ba de dag thams cad mthong // sangs rgyas la ni gshegs pa med/

117b2(phal chen): dmigs pa kun tu yang // sangs rgyas rgyal ba gshegs par brjod // 'jig rten khams rnams 'di dag ni// sangs rgyas sku rnams bdag gi med // sems la bdag gi meng pa bstan// byang chub rtogs la bdag gi

117b7(phal chen): te/ thams cad ni sangs rgyas gshegs// shing rnams kun tu rab tu snang // sangs rgyas sku ni thams cad// byin gyi rlabs dag rab tu 'thung // 'tshang rgya chos kyi 'khor lo dang // bsam pa bzhin du mya ngan 'dal/

119a3(phal chen): lngar bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad 'di'i sngon gyi smon lam dang / sngon gyi byin gyi rlabs dang / khyod kyi ye shes rnam par dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsabs brtan pa'i phyir/ 'di lta ste/ 
119a4(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i mi 'jigs pa rnam par dag par bya ba dang / spobs pa cha gas pa med par bya ba dang / ye shes kyis bsgribs pa med pa'i sar 'jug par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i sems yangs
119a5(phal chen): ba la rab tu 'jug par bya ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba mi za pa phun sum tshogs par bya ba dang / bsgribs pa med pa'i chos dkar po yongs gas par bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings la sgo kun nas 'jug
119a6(phal chen): par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi cho 'phrul bstan par bya ba dang / sngon gyi mtha'i mur thug pa'i ye shes dang dran pa rgyun mi chod par rnam par dag par bya ba dang / dbang po sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byin gyi rlabs

124b6(phal chen): 'di dag kun thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems rab tu snang bas 'khor ba'i dgon pa rgal dka' ba ras gdon par bya'o// g.yang sa chen po nas blangs par bya'o// gnod pa thams cad yongs dgrol bar bya'o// 
124b7(phal chen): 'khor ba'i rgyud las rab tu bsgral bar bya'o// bdag nyid kyis sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal gyi phung po blang bar spro bar bya'o// bdag gis sems can de dag thams cad 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal
124b8(phal chen): chenatha sa'i 'ogabs drang bar bya'o// 'jig rten gyi khams kyi mthar drug pa thams cad kyi ngan song kun gyi sdug bsngal thams cad blangs te/ khams myong bar bya ba la bdag gi spob bya'o// ngas tu
125a1(phal chen): sems can thams cad dge ba'i rtsa ba las mi spang bar sems can thams cad yongasu dgrol ba'i phyir bdag ngan song gcig na/ phyi ma'i mthar thug pa'i bskal par gnas par sprob
125a2(phal chen): bya'o// ngan song gcig tu ji lta ba de bzhin du/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad gtogs pa'i ngan song thams cad gnas par spro bar bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ kyi hung sems can 'di dag thams cad sdug bsngal
125a3(phal chen): gyi gan su lhung ba bas ni bdag gcig pu sdug bsngal myong yang blas/ bdag gis der bdag cing gtar bcug ste/ sems can dmyal ba dang / byol song gi skye gnas dang // gshin rje'i 'jig rten gyi dben pa
125a4(phal chen): ras 'gro ba thams cad brus te/ bdag gis sems can thams cad kyi don du sdug bsngal tshor ba'i phung po 'di dag thams cad bdag gi lus 'dis myong bar bya'o// bdag gis ni sems can rnams kyi gca'
125a5(phal chen): bden par smra ba dang / ying ches shing mi slu bar spro bar bya'i// bdag la rnaMs mas can thams cad kyis ma yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/  lha ste/ 'gro ba thams cad yongasu dgrol ba'i phyir/ bdag
125a6(phal chen): gis thams cad mkhyen pa'i sems sems can thams cad la dmigs pa skyes te/ bdag cid 'dod pa'i phyir ni blan meng pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu ma zhug so// 'dod pa'i yod tan lnga la dga' zhing
125a7(phal chen): spyod pa'i phyir yang ba yin// 'dod pa'i yul la bsnyen pa'i phyir yang ma yin// 'dod pa'i kham su gtogs pa'i dka' ba mang po gzhan blangs pa'i phyir yang byang chub kyi spyod pa la mi spyod // de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 
125a8(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi dga' ba 'di thams cad ni dgra yino// 'dod pa la brten pa 'di ni bdud kyi yulo// 'dod pa la brten pa de ni blo ngan pas bstar pa'i lam mo// sangs rgyas thams cad kyis spang ba'i yulo// de dag la rten
125b1(phal chen): pa de las sdug bsngal thams cad 'byung bar 'gyuraro// de las sems can dmyal ba dang / byol song gi skye gnas dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten 'di dag thams cad kyang 'byung bar 'gyuraro// de las sems can rnams
125b2(phal chen): 'thab pa dang / 'tshaya dru ba dang / rtsod pa dang / gnang la 'bebs pa dang / 'khrugs pa dang kun tu 'khrug pa rnams kyang rab tu 'byung // sems can 'di dag ni 'dod pa brten pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rngam
125b3(phal chen): las ring du gyur pa ste/ 'dong ba de dag ri mtho ris skye ba la yang bar du gcod ra/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub lta la smos kyang ci dgos te/ sems can thams cad kyi bde ba dang / dga' ba thams cad
125b4(phal chen): kyi yang bar chad 'gyur ro// de ltar bdag gis 'dod pa ni ro chung zhing tshad med pa'i nyes pa can du mthong na/ ci de yang de dag spyod pa'i phyir 'jug pa/ ma/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ bdag ni don 'di dag gi phyir bla na med pa
125b5(phal chen): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu zhugs pa ma yino// 'dod pa lang ga' ba'i phyir yang byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la mi spyod de/ de bas na/ sems can thams cad la phan pa dang / bde
125b6(phal chen): bar zhugs pa'i sems bskyed/ bdag ni 'di ltar sems cad thams cad kyi don gyi phyir/ de dag nyid kyi smon lam yongasu rdzogs par bya ba dang / bsngo zhing bsgrub pa'i phyir don de la zhugs pa ste/ de bas na/ 
125b7(phal chen): bdag gis sems can sdug bsngal gyi zhags pas bcings pa thams cad kyi sdug bsngal gyi zhags pa bcing / sdug bsngal thams cad las yongasu dgrol bar bya'o// sdug bsngal gyi rlung las rnam par
125b8(phal chen): bzlog par bya'o// bdag gis ji lta ji ltar sems can 'di dag thams cad shin tu bang ba dang / phan par 'gyur ba'i bde ba dang / tshor ba med pa'i bde ba dang / ni bo'i bde ba dang / mi gnas pa'i bde ba
126a1(phal chen): / dang mi g.yo ba'i bde ba dang / chang med pa'i bde ba dang / mnyams pa'i bde ba dang / mi 'gag pa'i bde ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi bang ba la rab tu thob par 'gyur ba des
126a2(phal chen): de ltar dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag yongasu bsngo bar bya'o// bdag kha lo sgyur ba dang / bdag mgon po dang / bdag me sgron 'dzin pa dang / bdag lam bde ba ston pa dang / bdag khom pa rnyed pa dang / bdag thabs la
126a3(phal chen): mkhas pa dang / bdag don shes pa dang / bdag 'khor ba'i rgya mtsho la thams cad mkhyen pa'i gru bo che'i mnyan par gyur pa dang / bdag yongasu bsngo ba la mkhas pa dang / bdag pha rol ston pas/ dge ba'i rtsa bde
126a4(phal chen): ngag ji lta ji ltar sems can rnams kyi skyab su 'gyur ba dang / 'khor bar gyur pa rnams yongs rgal bar 'gyur ba dang / de bzhin gsheg/ sa pa thams cad mnyes par 'gyur ba dang / thams cad mkhyen
126a5(phal chen): banyi du bsgribs pa med par 'gyur ba dang / bdud kyi yul rnams la mig nas par 'gyur ba dang / sdig pa mi dge ba'i grogs po tha yongasu spong bar 'gyur ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen byang chub
126a6(phal chen): sems dpa' sems dpa' thams cad la brten par 'gyur ba dang / las rnam par dag pa la kha na ma tho ba med par 'gyur ba dang / spyad pa chen po'i smon lam rnams yang dag par sgrub par 'gyur ba dang / dge ba'i
126a7(phal chen): rtsa ba thams cad khong du chud par 'gyur ba de lta de ltar yongasu bsngo'o// de la byang chub sems dpa' dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag yong su bsngo na/ sems 'di snyam du bskyed/ kye ma gling bzhi'i 'jig rten gyi khams snang bar
126a8(phal chen): bya ba'i phyir/ gling bzhi'i 'jig rten gyi khams na/ sems can ji snyed pa de snyed kyi nyi ma ni mi 'char gyi/ gling bzhi'i 'jig rten snang bar bya ba'i phyir khyi ma 'di nyid gcig pu 'char te/ sems can gling bzhir gtogs
126b1(phal chen): ba de dag rang rang gi lus las kyang snang ba gang gis de dag gi nyi ma'i grangs shes par 'gyur ba 'am/ rang gi don bsgrub par 'gyur ba 'am/ lo tog yongasu smin par 'gyur ba 'am/ nyin cig nyin cig cing bza' shing
126b2(phal chen): gi ra ba dang / grong khyer dag tu dga' ba dang / rtse ba'i longs spyod myong bar 'gyur ba 'am/ phyogs snang bar 'gyur ba 'am/ grong dang / grong khyer dang / ljongs dang / pho brang 'khor dang / rgyal po'i gnas ngag tu
126b3(phal chen): 'gro ba dang / 'ong bar bya ba 'am/ spyod pa'i doran sbyar bar bya ba'i sdang ba mi 'byung ste/ sems can de dag rang rang gi lus la yang 'ong gang gis de dag gi don bsgrub pa'i 'ong nga lta bu mi gtong ste/ 'di ltar lha'i
126b4(phal chen): nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor gcig pu gnyi su med pa de ni gling bzhi'i 'jig rten gyi khamasu sems can rnams la snang bar bya ba'i phyir 'char zhing rab tu 'byung // de bzhin du/ byang chub sems dpa' dge ba'i rtsab
126b5(phal chen): yongasu bsngo ba na/ sems 'di ltar skyes te/ sems can 'di dag tham sa cang la gang gis de dag bdag nyid yongasu bskyab par bya ba de nyid kyang med na/ gzhan bskyab pa lta ci smos kyis bdag
126b6(phal chen): nyid gcig pu gci su med pas/ sems can thams cad kyi phyir 'di ltar sems can thams cad dgrol ba dang / sems can thams cad snang bar bya ba dang / sems can thams cad gsal bar bya ba dang / sen

127a1(phal chen): dkyil 'khor de lta bur byas te/ gzhan las phan pa'i lar re bas bya'o// gzhan gyis skabs mi rnyed par bya'o// sems can thams cad kyi phyir go cha mi dor bar bya'o// sems can thams

127a4(phal chen): bar chags pa med pa'i chos ljid la brten te/ yongasu bsngo bar bya'o// sems can rnams kyi ngo bo grong yongasu bsngo bar bya'o// sa te/ de ni 'pho ba'i tshul gyis yongasu bsngo ba la gnas pa ma yin/

130a1(phal chen): ldan pa zhes bya ba gnyis pa gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' 'di lta ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyes par bya ba'i phyir/ sangs rgyas 'das pa dang / 
130a2(phal chen): ma byor pa dang / nga ltar byung ba'i thams cad la mi byed par dang ba yin// 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba dang / rgyud kyi tshul gcig par bya ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa
130a3(phal chen): nyi du sems bskyed pa gcig pa thob pa yan chad/ kun la yang mi byed par dang par yin/ 'di lta ste/ lhag pa'i bsam pas rab tu zhugs pa/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la mi phyed par dang pa yin/ 'di lta ste/ de bzhi/ 
130a4(phal chen): gshegs pa thams cad kyi bstan pa yang dag par gzung zhing bsrung ba'i phyir/ de dag dang de dag tu skyes pa'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bstan pa la mi phyed par dad pa yin/ 'di lta ste/ sdang ba med pa'i mig rab tu 'thob
130a5(phal chen): pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi don du dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongasusngo ba'i phyir/ sems can thams cad la mi byed par dang ba yin/ 'di lta ste/ mtha' yas pa'i dge ba'i rtsab mngon pa 'dubya
130a6(phal chen): shing yang dag par bsgrub pa'i phyir/ chos dkar po thams cad la mi phyed bar dang ba yin/ 'od lnga ste/ lhag pa'i bsam pa dang / mos pa yong sudu rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi yong su bsngob
130a7(phal chen): la mi byed par dad ba yin/ 'di lta ste/ ston pa'i 'du shes yongasu ma rgyas pa rgyas par bya ba'i phyir/ chos smra ba'i byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la mi byed par dad pa yin/ 'di lta ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa
130a8(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab pa la dang par bya ba'i phyir/ sangs pad kyi rnam par 'phrul pa dang / cho 'phrul la mi phyed par dad pa yin/ byang chub sems dpa'i thabs mkhas pa'i spyod pa rnam pa tha dad pa sna tshogs kyis
130b1(phal chen): yang dag par bzung ba/ dmigs pa kun tu rgyu ba gzhan dang gzhan can de dag thams cad la mi byed par dad pa yin te/ de ltar mi byed pa'i gnas rab tu thob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni dge ba'i rtsa ba ci'ang
130b2(phal chen): rung ste/ sangs rgyas sam/ byang chub sems dpa' 'am/ can thos sam/ rang sangs rgyas sam/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'am/ sems can rnams la dmigs pa gang dge ba'i rtsa ba sna tshogs sam/ dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam pa
130b3(phal chen): dad pa'am/ byang chub tu sems bskyed pa rnam par 'phel bar bya ba 'am/ byams pa bsgom pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba yang dag par bskyed pas kyang rung ste/ snying rje chen po yangs pa tshad med pa yang dag par mthong bas byang chub
130b4(phal chen): tu sems bskyed pa yangs par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rjesu pa sgrub pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rje su nan tan bya ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yang dag par bsdu ba dang / don shes
130b5(phal chen): pa la yang dag par 'jug par bya ba dang / bsod nams kyi tshogs yang nga ga par bsgrub pa dang / sbyin ba'i tshogs rab tu brtsam pa dang / yon tan thams cad kyi tshogs la rab tu 'jug par bya ba dang / 
130b6(phal chen): dus gsum mkham pa ci du rnam par dpyong pa byed cing / de dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag thams cad ma byed pa'i tshogs bsags pa'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// sangs rgyas thams cad blta ba dang / mi 'bral ba yongasu rdzogs par bya/ 
130b7(phal chen): ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad dang mi 'bral ba rab tu thob par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad dang mi 'bral bar 'grogs pa dang / thams cad mkhyen par sems bskyed pa yid
130b8(phal chen): la bya ba dang mi 'bral ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bstan pa yang dag par bzung zhing bsrung ba dang mi 'bral ba dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad yongasu smin par bya ba dang mi 'bral ba dang / 
131a1(phal chen): 'jig rten las 'das par sems bskyed cing / yongasu bsngo ba dang mi 'bral ba dang / chos smra ba thams cad la phu dung du bya ba dang mi 'bral ba dang / chos kyi snang ba thams cad thob
131a2(phal chen): ba dang mi 'bral ba dang / smon lam chen po la rab tu brtson par bya ba dang mi 'bral bar yong su bsngo'o// de ltar byang chub sems dpa' dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag yang dag par sgrub cing / yang dag par sdud pa dang / nye bar
131a3(phal chen): sogs pa dang / mngon par 'du byed pa dang / sems pa dang / dmigs par byed pa dang / rab tu rtog pa dang / yang dag par smon pa dang / kun tu spyod pa dang / nye bar ston pa'i tshe/ 'di ltar yongasu bsngo ste/ dge
131a4(phal chen): ba'i rtsa ba 'di dag 'di ltar bsgrubs pa las dge ba'i rtsa ba dang / rgyu 'thun pa'i 'bras bu gang byung ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba dang / rgyu 'thun pa'i 'bras bu des bdag byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa na/ sems kyi
131a5(phal chen): skad cig re re la brjod du med pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam sa mthong bar gyur cig/ de dag kyang mnyes par byas par gyur cig/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang / 
131a6(phal chen): par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de dag la yang sangs rgyas kyi rim gro d+ha chen po byas par gyur cig/ rin po che grangs med pa dang / me tog grangs med pa dang / dri grangs med pa dang / phreng ba grangs med pa dang / na
131a7(phal chen): grangs med pa dang / gdugs grangs med pa dang / rgyal mtshan grangs med po dang / ba dan grangs med pa dang / rgyan grangs med pa dang / lhab lhub grangs med pa dang / rim gro grangs med pa dang / byug ba grangs
131a8(phal chen): med pa dang / rnam par byug pa grangs med pa dang / me tog thams cad kyi gdan grangs med pa dang / spos thams cad kyi gdan grangs med pa dang / phreng ba thams cad kyi gdan grangs med pa dang / tsan dan bzang
131b1(phal chen): po thams cad kyi gangan grangs med pa dang / gos thams cad kyi gdan grangs med pa dang / rdo rje thams cad kyi gdan grangs med pa dang / nor bu rin po che thams cad kyi gdan grangs med pa dang / ring po che'i srang lem
131b2(phal chen): thams cad kyi gdan grangs med pa dang / rin po che'i kha dog gi gdan grangs med pa dang / rin po che thams cad kyi 'chag sa grangs med pa dang / me tog thams cad kyi 'chags grangs med pa dang / spos thams cad kyi
131b3(phal chen): 'chag sa grangs med pa dang / phreng ba'i rgyan thams cad kyi 'chag sa grangs med pa dang / gos thams cad kyi 'chag sa grangs med pa dang / rin po che thams cad kyis sna tshog su smras pa'i 'chag sa grangs med
131b4(phal chen): ba dang / rin po che thams cad kyi spang leb bting ba'i 'chags grangs med pa dang / rin po che thams cad kyi shing ta la'i 'phreng ba bsgreng ba'i 'chag sa grangs med pa dang / ring po che'i stegs bus bskor
131b5(phal chen): ba'i 'chags grangs med pa dang / ring po che thams cad kyi dril bu'idra bas kun nas log par byas pa'i 'chags grangs med pa dang lha rdzas thams cad las shin tu 'das pa'i dzi
131b6(phal chen): gtsug lag khang grangs med pa dang / lha rdzas thams cad las shin tu 'das pa'i me tog thams cad kyi gtsug lag khang grangs med pa dang / lha rdzas las shin tu 'das pa'i spos thams cad kyi gtsug lag
131b7(phal chen): sa grangs med pa dang /  rbab las shin tu 'das pa'i phreng ba rnams cad kyi banugs pa 'ang grangs med pa dang / sgra rdzas las shin tu 'das pa'i chang dang thams cad cigasugal ka khang bras
131b8(phal chen): pa rgya rdzas las shi du las pa'i chos dang dus pa mchog das pa thams cad kyi mazug lag yang grangs med pa dang / la rdzas thams cad las gan tu 'das pa'i rdo rje'i gtsug las 'a sa
132a1(phal chen): med pa dang / nor bu ring po che'i gtsug lag khang grangs med pa dang / spos kyi shing dang / gos kyi shing dang / rol mo'i shing dang / rin po che'i shing dang / lhab lhub kyi shing dang / shing
132a2(phal chen): sna tshogs kyis kun nas bskor ba'i gtsug lag khang grangs med pa dang / yid du 'ong ba'i sgra 'byung ba'i shing grangs med pa dang / snam bu rin po che sbyangs pa'i shing grangs med pa dang / rin po che mang po'i shing grangs
132a3(phal chen): med pa dang / me tog dang / phreng ba dang / spos dang / byug pa dang / gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan thams cad grangs med pa dang / shing thams cad kyis brgyan pa'i gtsug lag khang grangs med pa dang / ba gam gyi rgyan
132a4(phal chen): grangs med pa dang / skar khung gi brgyan grangs med pa dang / rta babs kyi rgyan grangs med pa dang / bu shu'i rgyan dang / zla gam gyi rgyan dang / khang pa brtsegs pa'i rgyan dang / bla re'i rgyan grangs med pa dang / gser
132a5(phal chen): gyi dra ba'i khab grangs med pa dang / spos dang / bdug pa'i dam pa tham sa cad kyi rgyan grangs med pa dang / gos thams cad gding bar bting ba'i rgyan gyis thams cad rab tu rgyan pa'i gtsug
132a6(phal chen): lag khang grangs med pas bsnyen bkur byas par gyur cig/ de ltar mchod pa rgya chen po sbyar te/ sangs rgyas thams cad la yid kyi dbang po shin tu dad pas mchod pa dang / rim gro rgyun mi chad pa/ sangs rgyas
132a7(phal chen): bu dung ngu bya ba dang / phyir mi ldog pa las thung bas phyag 'tshal zhing mchod pa dang / bsnyen bkur byas te/ de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad rim gror bya bas/ bskal pa brjo me 'i ma cwo 'a ca
132a8(phal chen): cig/ 'gro ba thams cad dang bar bya ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba yang dag par bsdu ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi sdug bsngal gyi phung po rnam par bzlog pa dang / sems rgya chen po
132b1(phal chen): bskyed pa la mos par bya ba dang / rgyan chen pos yang dag par brgyan pa dang / tshad med par rnam par bri ba'i rgyan dang / brtsams pa mthar phyin par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas 'byung ba shin tu dkon pa brjod par bya ba
132b2(phal chen): dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs yongasu rdzogs par bya ba dang / mchod rten sna tshogs bsnyen bkur bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bstan pa yang dag par gzung ba'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pa
132b3(phal chen): bcugs shing 'tsho skyong ba de la de lta bu'i rim gro byed pa dang / de dag yongasu mya ngan las 'das nas kyang sangs rgyas de dag thams cad kyi sku gdung mchod pa la rab tu brtson par bya bas bskal pa grangs med pa
132b4(phal chen): zad kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa de dag mchod pa dang / bsnyen bkur ba'i rgyan dang / brjod pa yon tan mtha' yas pa bsngags pas ba sgrubs pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad yongasu smin par bya
132b5(phal chen): bar bsgrubs pa de dag mthar thug par ma gyur cig/ de ltar rim gro byed ba las phyir ldog par ma gyur cig/ rgyun gcod par ma gyur tsog/ sems yongasu skyo ba med pa yang thod par gyur cig/ 
132b6(phal chen): mngon par chags pa med pa'i sems 'du shes rnam par spangs pa dang / mi gnas pa'i chos nyid dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba rlom sems thams cad bcom pas/ rlom sems med par gyur pa dang / chos 'gyur ba med
132b7(phal chen): ba yang dag par ji lta ba bzhin gyi rgyas btab pa'i chos kyi sgo dang / tshe dang skye ba thams cad du 'khor bar gyur pa'i sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa dang / skye ba med pa'i rang bzhin la dpyod cing dmigs pa'i chos kyi
132b8(phal chen): rgyas btab pa'i sems bskyed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pas byin gyis brlabs pa'i yongasu bsngo ba dang / chos kyi rang bzhin la rab tu brtson pa'i yongasu bsngo ba mnyam pa nyid dang / mngon par 'du bya ba
133a1(phal chen): med pa'i tshul la zhugs pa'i mngon par 'du bya ba med par sgrub pa dang / dngos po thams cad kyi 'du shes dang bral ba'i bsngo ba'i tshul dang / bsngo ba la mkhas pa'i rnam pa tshad med pa
133a2(phal chen): dang / byang chub sems dpa'i bsngo ba srid pa kun las 'phags pa dang / bsgom pa'i sgo mtshan ma la mkhas pas gnas pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba le bar len pa'i byin gyis rlabs
133a3(phal chen): can dang / byang chub tu sems bskyed pa bsngo ba chen pos yongasu sbyongs pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad la gnas pa'i mos pa yongasu rgyas par gnas thams cad yang dag par bcom par gyur cig/ de ltar
133a4(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag 'di ltar ci nas kyang 'khor ba'i rgyung du chud zos par mi 'gyur ba dang // ci nas kyang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyi du sems bskyed pa
133a5(phal chen): chud zos par mi 'gyur ba dang / ci nas kyang / srid pa'i 'du 'jis chus zos par mi 'gyur ba dang / ci nas kyang / sems can gyi kham sa thams cad bsgral ba dang / ci nas kyang skye ba dang / 
133a6(phal chen): 'chi 'phos skyon du mi 'gyur ba dang / ci nas kyang / chags pa med pa'i ye shes kyi sgo stong bar mi 'gyur ba dang / ci nas kyang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa'i rgyu zad par ma
133a7(phal chen): 'gyur ba dang / cinas kyang / 'jig rten gyi chos kyis kun tu blangs par mi 'gyur ba dang / ci nas kyang / pha rol tu phyid pa rnams kyis rnam par dag par 'gyor pa dang / ci nas kyang / thams cad mekhyen par
133a8(phal chen): stobs phun sum tshogs par 'gyur bar yongasu bsngo ste/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byang chub sems dpa'i sems bskyed pa mun pa med pa dang ldan pa ni/ chos dkar po snang bar gyur
133b1(phal chen): bas pangar brtan cing yong su bsngo ba'i mchog skyes bungs pas spyad pa dang ldan pa dang / yongasu dag pa'i yid kyis yang dag par rtog pa dang / sems dang 'dra ba'i chos thams cad la zhugs pa dang / snum
133b2(phal chen): dang 'dra ba'i las yongasu shes pa dang / mig yod lta bu'i las kyi rnam par smin pa la mos pa dang / sprul pa lta bu'i mngon par 'du byed pa la gnas pa dang / sgra brnyan lta bu'i las la brten pa dang / grib ma
133b3(phal chen): lta bu'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i rjes song ba dang / chags pa med pa'i chos kyi mig rab tu skyes pa dang / bya ba med par 'byam klas pa'i rjesu song ba dang / zhi ba'i rigs rab tu thob pa dang / gzhi su med pa dang
133b4(phal chen): ldan pa'i 'dus byas dang / 'dus ma byas kyi chos thams cad la rab tu chu gas pa dang / chos ma nor ba'i mtshan ma thob par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad kyi rjesu song ba dang / mtshan
133b5(phal chen): ma thams cad la zhen pa med pa dang / thun mong gi las la mkhas pa'i rjesu song ba dang / chos dkar po thams cad rgyun ma chad pa dang / chags pa thams cad kyis mngon par ma zhen pa dang / 
133b6(phal chen): chags pa med par 'gro ba la brten pa dang ldan pa yin te/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gan tu sra pa'i blo dang ldan pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba la rmongs pa med pa/ chos thams cad dang 'gal ba med
133b7(phal chen): ba'i chos can rgyu dang las dang bya ba dang / 'gal ba med pa yang dag par mthong ba yongasu bsngo ba la mkhas pa/ ngan cid kyi chos kyi tshul dang / las rnam par smid pa mngon par bsgrub pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa chos
133b8(phal chen): thams cad la rnam par lta zhing / rnam par dpyod pa'i ye shes dang ldan pa yongasu bsngo ba'i ye shes chen po mngon par shes pa las shin tu rig pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba dang ldan pa mngon par 'du bya ba med par
134a1(phal chen): spyong pa'i sems dge ba dang ldan pa de dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag 'di ltar ci nas kyang / 'gro ba thams cad yongasu dgrol ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi rigs bdud kyi las dang bral ba las
134a2(phal chen): kyi rnam pa yongs byung ba'i bdag nyid can thams cad mkhyen pa nyi du mos shing rjesu song ba'i sems dang ldan par 'gyur bar yongasu bsngo'o// bsngo ba de yang tshad med pa'i ye shes khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir/ 
134a3(phal chen): yang dag par mthong bar byed de/ dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag 'jig rten gyi yul dang rnam par bral ba/ nyon mongs pa thams cad dang rnam par bral bar yong su bsngo'o// sems can thams cad shin tu rnam par byang ba'i
134a4(phal chen): phyir yang yongasu bsngo ste/ ye shes rnam par dag pa'i mthar thug par zab pa'i tshul gyis dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag ci nas kyang / 'khor ba'i chos kyis mi bskyod cing / sangs rgyas kyi dge ba mngon par

134a6(phal chen): yongasu bsngo ba'i ye shes kyi rjesu song ba las rgyas 'debs par byed// dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi longs spyod kyi phyir yang / chos thams cad 'jig rten las 'das par khong du chud pa'i

134a8(phal chen): ba'i rtsa ba dang ldan pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yongasu bsngo ba mi phyed pa dang ldan pa zhes bya ba ste gnyis pa'o// yongasu bsngo ba de dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' na

134b2(phal chen): du rung bar bye // chos thams cad la 'jug pa rmongs pa med pa la yang rab tu 'jug/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byin gyi rlabs bdud kyi las thams cad rab tu 'jom pa yang yongasu smra'o// mngon par skyes pa'i
134b3(phal chen): byang chub kyi sems kyang yong su rdzogs par 'grub par 'gyuraro// chags pa med pa la rab tu 'jug pa'i phyir gzhar gyi drong mi 'jog pa 'ang yang dag par 'gru'o// chos thams cad kyi don mthong sarab tu 'thob// sangs
134b4(phal chen): kyi zhing thams cad kyi rje'u song ba'i 'du shes kyi gnas kyang rab tu rtogs par byed// 'gro ba thams cad yongasu spang bar bya ba'i yongasu dag pa yang yong su bsgru'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan
134b5(phal chen): gyis sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshig su bcad pa 'di dag smraso// de dag yid ni dbye ba ma nga bsgyur cing // ji sbed las rnams yang dag brtson byed ku
134b6(phal chen): ci nas rgyal ba mngon bar mnyes 'gyur ba// de ltar 'jig rten mkhas la yongasu bsngo ba byed// sangs rgyas bsam du med pa bsnyen bkur cing // sbyin 'dul sdom pa mchog gi tshul khrims rnams// ci nas 'gro kur
134b7(phal chen): bar dag 'gyur ba// de ltar 'jig rten par phyir yongasu bsngo// ji sbed 'din spos kyi gzhol med khang // me tog rnam pa na bza'i rnam pa dang / lha'i lhub rnam pa gdugs kyi rnam pa dag/ des ni ye shes mkhas la bsnyen
134b8(phal chen): bkur byed// de ltar skyes bu'i seng ge drang srong rnams// bskal pa bsam yas bsnyen cing bkur byas kyang // rgyal ba skyes bu 'dul ba mchod byas pas// nam yang ngoms par tshor bar mi 'gyu ro// de dag rgyal ba kun
135a1(phal chen): mos byed cing // phyogs rnams kun gyi 'jig rten sgron ma'i rnams// mi'i seng ge'i mtshungs med ji skyed// 'jig rten phyogs bcu dag na bzhugs pa mthong // bskal ba bsam gyis mi
135a2(phal chen): rnam mang du// mi ngoms yid kyis sbyin pa gtong byed cing // dge ba de la rjesu sems byed pas// bskal pa brgyar yang ngoms par mi tshor ro// 'gro ba'i 'du shes rnam rtog rab shes kyang // de la de ni mi rtog rnam mi rtag/ 
135a3(phal chen): de dag 'gro ba'i dbang po ma lus shes// de dag phan phyir rtag tu 'jug par byed// de dag dga' zhing mnyam par gzhag pa'i sems// dad pa 'od gsal sri zhu ldan pa'i rnams// bsam yas bskal par 'jig rten
135a4(phal chen): 'gro ban phyir// yongasu dgrol ba'i sems kyis spro bar byed// de dag bde gshegs mya ngan 'das pa la// sna tshogs rnam pa tha dad yid 'ong ba'i// mchod rten bsam gyis mi khyab rtsig byed kyi// mchod pa byed kyang
135a5(phal chen): nam yang tshim pa med// mtshungs med de dag sku gzugs rnam dag pa// rab tu 'od 'bar gser gyi snying po can// rgyal ba'i sku gzugs ri rab mnyam pa dag/ bye ba brgya phrag mtha' yas rab tu byed/ 
135a6(phal chen): zil gnon ngas pa rnyed pa de dag ni// bsod nams yangs pa'i stobs de sgrub pa na// de dag yongs bsngo shes pa rab rtogs shing // dngos dang dngos med thams cad rab tu bsgom// 'di 'dra'i ye shes tshul la

157b3(phal chen): can gang yang 'khor ba med// sems can 'byung ba de dag mi byed de// sems can rnams la gnas pa med par smras// sems can rgyud kyis brda' yang rab tu rtogs// bsod nams mi zad pa'i
157b4(phal chen): mdzod ces bya ba ste yongasu bsngo ba lnga pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyis yongasu bsngo ba drug pa dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid kyi rjesu song ba
157b5(phal chen): zhes bya ba gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras ngag 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rgyal por gyur te/ sring chen po thob nas 'a tshe ba dang phyir rgol ba bcom ste/ rgyal po chen por grags pa
157b6(phal chen): dang / srid chen po'i khams la gnas shing // sring yangs pa la dbang bar gyur nas/ khon med cing ltong pa med par srid la gnas pa/ chos kyi rgyal srid kyis sbyong bar byed pa/ chos dang 'thun pa/ chos kyi rjesu
157b7(phal chen): snyegs pa/ phur sum tshogs pa'i srid chen po thob pa// sa chen po la gdugs cig tu gyur pa/ 'khor lo thogs pa med pas skyong ba/ dri ma med pa'i thabs thob pa/ sring la pha rol gyi sdes gtse ba med pa/ chos dang

158a8(phal chen): bcings shing / btson ran 'dug pa'i sems can rnams mthong nas nor thams cad yongasu gtong ba dang / g.yog dang bdag tu bcas te/ byin nas btson ra de dag nas/ sems can rnams yongasu thar par byed pa/

159a8(phal chen): bzung ba/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyi snying po'i rjesu song bas 'du byed shin tu bzung ba/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyi snying po'i rjesu song bas/ rnam par shes pa shin tu bzung ba/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thang

179b4(phal chen): gyi rgyan gyis kun tu yog par bya ba'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// sangs rgyas kyi mtshan la mos pa'i sems can thams cad dang 'gro ba'i cho ga sa thams cad gdugs thams cad kyis dgab pa'i phyir
179b5(phal chen): yongasu bsngo'o// rin po che thams cad kyi gdugs sna tshogs brjod ma nga pa'i yang brjod med pas sangs rgyas gcig la phul bas/ sangs rgyas thams cad la brjod med pa'i gdugs phul
179b6(phal chen): sems shing yongasu bsngo'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byang chub mngon par byang chub pas/ 'phags pa'i gdugs kyis sangs rgyas thams cad dga' ba'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// sangs rgyas kyi sku ji snyed 'jig rten gyi
179b7(phal chen): khams chos kyi dbyings kyis klas/ mamakha'i mthas gtugs pa thams cad na bzhugs pa thams cad la gdugs kyis dgab pa'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// nor bu rin po che thams cad kyis brgyan pa'i gdugs dang
179b8(phal chen): rin po che thams cad kyi phreng ba brgyung shing klubs pa dang / spos thams cad kyi mchog gi dri zhim po'i ngang 'thung ba'i gdugs dang rin po che sna tshogs kyis rnam par smras pa'i gdugs dang / rgyan mdzes shing rnam
180a1(phal chen): pa ga pa'i gagrus dang / rgyan chang med par yangs shing rgya che ba dang / gser gyi drabs kun nas log par brgyan pa/ dril bu'i dra ba kun nas surgyas pa'i sgra yi 'ong shing ldan pa 'a
180a2(phal chen): ba'i gdugs dang / ye shes bsgribs pa med cing chags pa med pa'i gdugs dang / sangs rgyas thams cad la mngon par dga' ba'i gdugs yongasu btang ba'i phyir yongasu bsngo ste/ de ltar byang chub sems
180a3(phal chen): dpa' sems dpa' chen po gdugs kyi sbyin pas yang dag par gzung ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag sems can thams cad la ye shes mchog gis gdugs kyis mngon par dgab pa'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// sangs rgyas
180a4(phal chen): thams cad kyi yon tan gyis kun nas g.yogs shing rab tu brgyan pa'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// sangs rgyas kyi ye shes dang yon tan dang dgongs pa ngas pa rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// sems can
180a5(phal chen): po tsha mtha' yas pa la dbang sbyar ba rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir yong su bsngo'o// chos thams cad la ye shes kyi dbang smrar ba kun tu rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir long su bsngo'o// dge ba'i rtsab thams
180a6(phal chen): cad kyis mngon par g.yog par yongasu bsngo ba'i don du yongasu bsngo'o// 'gro ba thams cad kyi ye shes mchog gi gdugs rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi stobs bcus pa/ 
180a7(phal chen): bres pa'i gdugs su 'gyur bar bya ba'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// chos kyi dbyings thams cad sangs rgyas kyi zhing gcig gi g.yog par bya ba'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// chos thams cad la dbang phyug tu dbang sgyu
180a8(phal chen): ba'i dang thob par bya ba'i phyir yong du bsngo'o// mthu chen po dang dbang chen po'i sems kyi rgyud thob par bya ba'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// blo yangs pa dang sems rgya che ba thob par bya ba'i phyir yongasu brjem
180b1(phal chen): yom tan tshad med pas 'gro ba thams cad mngon par dgab pa'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// yon tan thams cad kyis sems mngon par dga' ba'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// sems can thams cad kyis 'gro ba thams cad bango
180b2(phal chen): bar dgab pa'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// ye shes chen pos mnyam par dgab pa thob par bya sa phyid yongasu bsngo'o// sems can thams cad kyi bsngo ba'i tshul ma lus par thob par bya ba'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// sems
180b3(phal chen): dang bsam pa rnam par dag par 'gyur ba'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// bsam pa dge ba dang yid kyi dbang po rnam par dag pa dang ldan par bya ba'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// 'gro ba thams cad yongasu bsngo ba chen pos mngon par
180b4(phal chen): dga' cing yang dag par bsdu ba'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// 'di ltar yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rgyal mchi na dang / ba dan rin po che sna tshogs rnam pa tha dad pa'i yu ba can rin po
180b5(phal chen): dril bu'i dra ba 'khrol ba'i sgra yid 'ong ba 'thung ba/ snam bu rin po che rnam pa sna tshogs dbyangs pa/ kha dog dang tshon sna tshogs kyi snam bus brgyan cing bsgreng ba/ gser gyi dra bas kun nas
180b6(phal chen): dbyangs shing klubs pa/ gser gyi dril bu'i sgra 'byung ba/ dril bu g.yer ka'i dra bas shin tu brgyan pa'i rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong kha dog tha dad pa/ tshon tha dad pa/ shin tu mtho
180b7(phal chen): rin po chos rnam pa sna tshogasu brgyan pa/ rgyal mtshan gyi rtse mo zla gam gyis mdzes par brgyan pa/ 'dzam+bu chu klung gi gser gyi nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor bcug pa/ 'od zer rnam pa sna tshogs 'byung ba/ rgyal mtshan
180b8(phal chen): gyi rgyan gyis sa thams cad kun tu yog pa/ rgyal mtshan gyi rgyan rnam pa du ma 'ong dang ldan pas rab tu brgyan pa'i rgyal mtshan rnam pa sna tshogs bsgreng ba'i rgyan de lta bu dag/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams sa
181a1(phal chen): kyi las kyi rnam par smin pa la mos pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi rgyan gyis kun tu khyab par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyis klas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing namakha'
181a2(phal chen): dbyings thams cad 'byam klas pa la gnas pa yangs pa/ kun du rgyal mtshan gyi sbyin pa yongasu btang bar mos pas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rgyas par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i bsamapa
181a3(phal chen): dang mos pa'i khyab par rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mngon du gyur pa rnams la 'bul ba 'am/ de bzhin gshegs pa yongasu mya ngan las 'das pa'i mchod rten nam/ 
181a4(phal chen): chos dkon mchog mchod pa 'am/ dge 'dun dkon mchog la 'bul lam/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen byang chub sems dpa' rnams sam/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas rnams sam/ 'khor gyi
181a5(phal chen): tshogasu gyur pa 'am/ gang zag gi rnam pa gzhan su yang rung ste/ slong ba tha mas cad la rim gror bye ba'i phyir/ sbyin zhing yongasu gtong ba na/ rgyal mtshan dang ba ngan sbyin pas yang dag par bsdus
181a6(phal chen): pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba 'di ltar yongasu bsngo ste/ dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis sems can thams cad ye shes kyi rgyal mtshan dang ba ngan la thub pa med pas/ dge ba'i rtsa ba dang bsod nams thams cad yang dag
181a7(phal chen): par bsgreng ba'i rgyal mtshan 'dugyur cig/ sems can thams cad chos kyi go 'phang bris pa sbeng pa'i chos nyid kyis chos thams cad la dbang sgyur ba'i rgyal mtshan bsgreng bar gyur cig/ sems can
181a8(phal chen): thams cad sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byang chub kyi chos yang dag par 'dzin pa'i chos can du gyur te/ rin po che'i gzhi la sangs rgyas kyi chos bros pa dang ldan par gyur cig/ sems can thams cad
181b1(phal chen): 'gro ba kun la mar me snang bar gyur te/ rgyal mtshar shin tu 'phags par gyur cig/ sems can thams cad bdud thams cad rnam par 'joms pa'i phyir/ thub pa med pa'i rgyal mtshan dang ba ngan car du gyur cig/ 
181b2(phal chen): sems can thams cad bdud thams cad kyis mi thub pa'i chos can du gyur te/ ye shes dang stobs kyi rgyal mtshan rab tu bsgreng bar gyur cig/ sems can thams cad rgyal mtshan thams cad mi ltung ba'i
181b3(phal chen): sA ba can du gyur te/ ye shes mthu bo che'i rgyal mtshan dang ldan par gyur cig/ sems can thams cad ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor gyis chos kyi dbyings thams cad rnam par dag par gyur te/ ye shes kyi
181b4(phal chen): ma'i dkyil 'khor 'od zer rab tu 'gyed pa'i rgyal mtshan dang ldan par gyur cig/ sems can thams cad sangs rgyas kyi mchod pa la brtson zhing rgyal mtshan sna tshogs rab tu bsgreng bas/ 
181b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ming brjod med pa rgyas par 'gengs pa'i phyir rin po che'i rgyal mtshan dang ldan par gyur cig/ sems can thams cad zhags pa thub pa dgu bcu rtsa drug gi rgyal
181b6(phal chen): mtshan gyis dben zhing sems 'dod chags dang bral bar gyur te/ sangs rgyas kyi rgyal mtshan rab tu thob par gyur cig ces/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rgyal mtshan dang ba dan
181b7(phal chen): gyi sbyin pa byed pa'i tshe/ dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag sems can thams cad byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgya che zhing yangs pa dang / zab mo thams cad dang ldan par bya ba'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// byang chub sems
181b8(phal chen): dpa' thams cad kyi spyod pa dang / rnam par 'phrul pa dang / 'byung ba'i rgyal mtshan dang ldan zhing tha dad pa/ yang dag par shes pa rnam par dag pa/ thob par bya ba'i phyir yongasu bsngo'o// 'di ltar
182a1(phal chen): yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rin po che thams cad gtong ba la mos pa dang / sems can thams cad nor gyis byug par byed pa dang / rin po che'i mdzod thams
182a2(phal chen): cang 'byed pa dang / rin po che thams cad gtong ba dang / rin po che'i 'byung gnas thams cad yongasu gtong ba dang / nor bu rin po che thams cad kyi sbyin pa byed pa dang / rin po che kun gyis sems can thams cad
182a3(phal chen): la khyab par byed pa dang / rin po che'i tsho gas thams cad phangs par mi sems pa'i yid kyis gtong ba dang / ring po che'i tshogs thams cad 'thor ba'am/ rin po che thams cad yongasu gtang bar
182a4(phal chen): sems bskyed pa'i tshe/ srog chags bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa la rin po che byin pas/ yongasu bzung ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag 'di ltar yongasu bsngo'o// sems can thams cad dran pa'i rgyud

182a7(phal chen): bar dag pas/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems rin po che rab tu thob par gyur cig/ sems can thams cad sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la rmongs pa med par gzhol bas/ ye shes rin po che la

182b1(phal chen): cig/ sems can thams cad stobs bcu'i ye shes rin po che mngon par 'tshang rgya ba la brtson pas yon tan rin po che mtha' yas pa'i bsngags pa dang ldan par gyur cig/ sems can thams cad ye shes rin po
